Current Commentary

Favorable Developments in European Diplomacy

— Hua

Since the signing of the Anglo-Italian Gentleman's Agreement regarding the Mediterranean last week, a similar agreement has also been reached between France and Italy. The tense atmosphere in the Mediterranean over the past year has surprisingly shown gradual improvement towards the end of the year. This improvement has now produced concrete results: Italy has changed its attitude towards the non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War, ceasing its support for the rebel forces in Spain. As for Germany, which continues its active intervention, it has been jointly advised by Britain and France.

This joint British and French stance on the issue of non-intervention in Spain is important not only for addressing the Spanish situation itself but also for the genuine cooperation between these two countries in diplomacy. Over the past year, Britain and France have consistently appeared to be cooperating superficially but not genuinely on many important European issues. For example, France's attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian issue was not as firm as Britain's, and Britain's attitude towards the Locarno issue was not as concerned as France's. This inconsistency in attitudes has actually been the cause of many European crises over the past year. However, in the past month or two, France has clearly been helping Britain in its negotiations with Italy. And in dealing with the Spanish issue, France has consistently adhered to a common stance with Britain. This diplomatic strategy has now achieved considerable success. Therefore, after the signing of the Gentleman's Agreement on the Mediterranean, Britain and France simultaneously issued warnings to Germany regarding its intervention in the Spanish Civil War. And such a joint warning is, in fact, equivalent to a very strong warning.

From this perspective, the diplomacy of the current French Popular Front government is clearly more successful than that of the Laval era. From Germany's announcement of its rearmament last year to its advance into the Rhineland this year, it has been the weakest period for French diplomatic power since the war. This time, French Foreign Minister Delbos's talks with the German ambassador have given a fairly tough warning regarding Germany's support for the Spanish rebels. This relatively forceful expression should be the prelude to France gradually restoring its original diplomatic position. Upon closer examination of Léon Blum's foreign policy, it seems that his approach is very good. On the one hand, he fully trusts the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact. On the other hand, he also insists on not abandoning cooperation with Britain. He even tries to maintain a compromise with Italy, whose policies contain some contradictions with French policies. In addition to seeking to further strengthen France's relations with the Little Entente countries, he also strives to restore the old friendship between Poland, which has been relatively estranged in recent years, and France. This diplomatic strategy has one central goal: to prevent the aggression of Germany, France's greatest enemy. The general development of the European diplomatic situation now proves that Léon Blum's diplomatic efforts have been somewhat able to achieve his goal.

Christmas Celebrations in Various Countries: Over a Hundred Deaths in Frivolous Celebrations in the United States; Former King Reads Scriptures in a Church in Vienna; Residents of Paris Flock to the Mountains for Winter Sports

(New York) The number of people who have died in the nationwide Christmas celebrations and revelry has reached 158, including 97 who died in car and train accidents. It is estimated that the number of deaths will exceed 300. (December 25, National Telegraph)

(London) King George VI, Queen Elizabeth, and other members of the royal family gathered at Sandringham House to spend the Christmas holiday in a simple and sincere atmosphere. The King and Queen first went to the local church to participate in religious ceremonies and then returned to Sandringham House. There, they were informed by Queen Mary that the Duchess of Kent had given birth to a daughter, filling the family with joy. The entire royal family then took their seats for a banquet. Afterwards, they received congratulations from the palace staff in the grand hall and distributed gifts. The Duke of Windsor, the former King, congratulated Queen Mary and his brothers via long-distance telephone from Vienna before midnight. (December 25, Havas)

(Paris) This year, during the Christmas holiday, residents of the capital flocked to the mountains for winter sports. The number of extra trains temporarily added to various train stations broke all previous records. For example, from 7:30 PM to midnight the day before yesterday, the "Lyon" station alone dispatched as many as 52 passenger trains, carrying a total of more than 30,000 passengers. Yesterday, passenger trains departed from various stations in the capital every three and a half minutes. Most passengers were traveling in groups, carrying skiing equipment, climbing into the carriages, jostling to get ahead. All seats on every train, from the most luxurious sleeping cars to third-class carriages, were fully booked more than ten days in advance. As for the streets near the stations, taxis were lined up in three rows, with dozens running. Passengers, fearing they would miss their trains, urged the drivers to honk their horns, the sound deafening. These passengers all carried skiing equipment, placed on top of the cars, as dense as a forest. This was truly a spectacular sight unprecedented in previous years. (December 25, Havas)

(Rome) Last year, during Christmas, it was shortly after the start of the Italian-Abyssinian War, and when various countries implemented sanctions against Italy, all celebrations were suspended. This year, with all worries relieved, celebrations were held enthusiastically. Members of the royal family went to the Savoy Palace to spend the Christmas holiday and enjoy family time. Prime Minister Mussolini also went to his hometown of Romagna to spend the holiday. This is the first time the Prime Minister has left the capital at the end of the year. (December 25, Havas)

Vatican City: After Pope Pius XI delivered his Christmas broadcast from his sickbed last night, he spent the night in good condition. Congratulatory telegrams from around the world arrived like snowflakes today. (December 25, National Telegraph)

(Vienna) The Duke of Windsor, the former King of England, preached in an English church here today, reading Luke's Gospel, chapters 1 to 20, about the birth of Jesus. The congregation was quite surprised, and this was the first time the Duke of Windsor had appeared in public since his abdication. When he read the Bible, his face was pale, but his pronunciation was clear and reverent, and the listeners were silent. The British and American ambassadors to Austria and their wives attended the service. (December 25, National Telegraph)

(London) Prime Minister Lloyd George today received a telegram from the Duke of Windsor, the former King, in response to his Christmas greetings: "I am deeply moved by your kind thoughts and greetings. I sincerely wish you happiness and blessings." Signed Edward. (December 26, Reuters)

(Vienna) When the Duke of Windsor learned today that the Duchess of Kent had given birth to a daughter, he was dining with the staff of the British Embassy to celebrate Christmas. Everyone present immediately raised their glasses to celebrate. (December 25, National Telegraph)

(London) The Duchess of Kent gave birth to a daughter today, and both mother and child are safe. The attending physician arrived at Bellevue House at 7:30 AM this morning, and Home Secretary Simon also arrived to await the birth. (December 25, National Telegraph)

(London) The Duchess of Kent gave birth to a daughter at 11:20 AM this morning, and both mother and child are safe. Queen Mary now has six grandchildren. The Duchess gave birth to a son on October 9th of last year, named Edward. The Duchess is the former Princess Marina of Greece, who married the Duke of Kent in London in 1934. The ceremony was exceptionally grand. (December 25, Reuters)

Soldiers on the Spanish Front Do Not Forget Christmas; Rebel Artillery and Aircraft Bomb the Capital; Great Panic Among Pedestrians in the Streets of Madrid

Madrid: The government army and militia today granted a rebel army officer permission to cross the "no man's land" between the two armies to spend Christmas with his family in the suburbs. (December 25, National Telegraph)

Avila: Yesterday was Christmas Day. The Carlist soldiers belonging to the Nationalist militia in the Guadarrama Mountains north of Madrid celebrated the holiday in their military quarters. The terrain there is high, 1,500 meters above sea level, surrounded by huge pine trees covered with snow. The soldiers sat on the ground, each bringing out food sent by relatives and the public, such as ham, sausages, poultry, cakes, and wine, scattered all over the ground, sitting around eating heartily. The army had no kitchen equipment, so they roasted turkeys on bayonets and then ate them. Candles were placed nearby, and pine needles were scattered above. In this solemn environment, they spent the holiday peacefully, while reconnaissance teams remained on guard at the front lines. (December 26, Havas)

Madrid: Today is Christmas Day. Nationalist artillery units heavily shelled Madrid amidst the ringing of church bells. At least 20 artillery shells landed near the telephone bureau, and many shells also landed in the Gran Vía area. Fires broke out in several places, and the sound of sirens filled the air as fire trucks rushed through the streets to put out the fires. Although several Nationalist artillery shells hit the telephone bureau, none of the staff inside were injured. (December 25, National Telegraph)

Madrid: Although today is Christmas Day, Nationalist forces continued to shell the capital for an hour. The main targets of the shelling were the Central Telephone Company building and the Stock Exchange. Both places were hit, with no fewer than thirty shells landing. Fortunately, the number of casualties was not very high. The first few shells landed on Gran Vía Avenue at 4 PM. The glass windows of several cafes were shattered. The weather was mild at the time, and there were many pedestrians on the street. When the shells landed, the crowd panicked and fled to the subway and the corridors of private residences. Women clutched babies in their arms, not knowing what to do. Several militiamen immediately rushed to the scene to restore order, ordering the crowd to evacuate to neighboring streets and protecting the area near the Central Telephone Company and the Stock Exchange. At 4:20 PM, a fire broke out on the upper floor of the Central Telephone Company building. Staff inside immediately extinguished the fire with fire extinguishers. Soon, firefighters arrived and put out the fire in a quarter of an hour. Several special correspondents from this newspaper were gathering inside the Central Telephone Company building at the time, conducting their daily interviews, and witnessed the situation. By 5 PM, the fire was completely extinguished. The facades of the Telephone Company and the Stock Exchange were destroyed by the fire, but telegraph and telephone communications with the rest of the world had not been interrupted. According to the latest news, three women and two men were killed and seriously injured in the incident. There were several interesting anecdotes during the incident. When the Telephone Company caught fire, a servant calmly washed the marble steps in front of the building, as if thinking that the steps had been trampled by firefighters and had to be cleaned immediately, while the sound of artillery fire outside was ignored. In the telephone switchboard room, a female telephone operator did not immediately evacuate to a safe place after hearing the alarm, but insisted on asking the manager for a pencil. The manager replied, "Forget it." Such anecdotes are common in the most serious incidents. (December 25, Havas)

Madrid: Although yesterday was Christmas Day, several Nationalist aircraft bombed the city again at 11 PM, dropping many bombs on the outskirts of the capital. It is reported that no fewer than ten bombs exploded. The extent of the damage is unknown. The government army immediately opened fire with anti-aircraft guns and repelled the aircraft. (December 26, Havas)

Prohibition of Volunteer Soldiers Enlisting in Spain; Britain and France to Negotiate with Various Countries Tomorrow; Hitler Considering Germany's Actions

(Paris) Responsible sources have stated that Britain and France will conduct negotiations with the governments of relevant countries on Monday of next week, requesting a ban on volunteer soldiers enlisting in Spain. However, no action has been taken so far. If the German government can prohibit its volunteer soldiers from enlisting in Spain and provide a promise to limit armaments, then Britain and France can provide economic benefits. (December 26, Havas)

(Paris) German leader Hitler is currently vacationing at his villa in Berchtesgaden, Germany. He is considering the opinions recently expressed by the French authorities. The diplomatic circles of various European countries are focusing on the city. Regarding this matter, Mrs. Tabouis, a diplomatic reporter, recently stated that before replying to the French government, Hitler asked Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, "Is Italy no longer intervening in the Spanish Civil War?" He will not make a decision until he receives a reply from the Italian Prime Minister. (December 26, Havas)

Bayonne, France: The German cargo ship Barlo, which was intercepted by a government warship in the waters of the Basque Autonomous Region of Spain the day before yesterday, was forced to sail to the port of Bayonne. Once it arrived at the port, the crew was detained. Regarding this matter, the authorities of the Basque Autonomous Region refused to release any information, including the contents of the ship. (December 25, Havas)

(Paris) Bertin, a famous reporter for the Paris Echo, recently stated that the attitude that the British and French governments should take towards Germany is to issue a statement to Berlin stating that "Germany's current policy of self-sufficiency is a reckless move. Its four-year plan must be abandoned, and it must work with us to allow Germany to rejoin the international community where capital, commerce, and services are connected. Germany's gold reserves are exhausted, and its deposits are also lacking. We will remedy this. We will also facilitate Germany's access to colonial raw materials needed by German producers, just as we do. We may go further and give Germany land outside of Europe, but with one condition: that we sincerely hope that Germany's current policies can be fundamentally changed and no longer openly prepare for aggression. On the contrary, provide concrete guarantees to show its determination to abide by international law." Bertin then concluded, "If Germany's self-sufficiency policy is to be eased, then Germany's socialist system may be weakened or even overturned." The Communist Party's newspaper "L'Humanité" stated, "Can Germany obtain colonies?" This is not impossible, but Germany must cease its intervention in the Spanish Civil War and not use this as an exchange condition. Can we say to German leader Hitler, "If you abandon your policy of intervening in the Spanish Civil War, we will give you colonies?" (December 26, Havas)

Germany Deploys Military Forces on the Swiss Border; Report by a French Reporter

(Paris) Boursier, a famous reporter for L'Intransigeant, recently described the military preparations being carried out by Germany in areas adjacent to the Swiss border, as well as the Swiss government's response. He stated that the holidays for the German National Defense Force and the Labor Service Corps during Christmas and New Year's have been canceled. Since the 13th of this month, members of the National Socialist Storm Troopers and the SS have been carrying machine guns and cannons, traveling by car to station themselves in the area of Lörrach in the southwestern border region, which is only seven kilometers away from Basel, Switzerland. "The railway from Stuttgart to Friedrichshafen, which originally passed through Basel, Switzerland, has now been rebuilt within the country, only five kilometers from Basel. A cave has been built on the shores of Lake Constance, fully loaded with bullets and explosives. All of this is due to the efforts of the Storm Troopers and the SS." The Swiss government feels threatened by this move by Germany and has begun preparations to respond. On the 4th of this month, a new company of volunteers was formed, consisting of engineers and unemployed workers from the reserve army, and is scheduled to be stationed in the city of Porrentruy in the north (twenty kilometers from the Jura region). The General Staff has also taken various measures to prepare to quickly form several volunteer teams. "In addition, all active-duty soldiers of the Swiss Army have been building trenches and fortifications along the Rhine River between Basel and Schaffhausen since the 21st of this month, but so far, nothing has been leaked to the outside world." (December 26, Havas)

Prime Minister of Southern Country Goes to Romania for Hunting; Also Discussing the Issues of the Little Entente

Bucharest, Romania: Yugoslav Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Stojadinović, at the invitation of the authorities, arrived at the Reşiţa train station today for hunting. Romanian Prime Minister Tătărescu and Foreign Minister Antonescu were at the station to welcome him. During the hunt, the three will discuss various issues related to the Little Entente. (December 26, Havas)

Opening of the Japanese Parliament; Compilation of the Next Budget; Finance Minister Announces Policy

(Tokyo) The opening ceremony of the 70th session of Parliament was held in the House of Peers this morning at 11 AM, with the Emperor personally attending. The Emperor wore an army-style dress uniform, rode in a royal carriage, and was escorted by a guard of honor of cavalry. He arrived at the main gate of the new Diet Building at 10:45 AM and entered the waiting room inside the Diet Building, where he met with various members of the imperial family, cabinet members, and the presidents and vice-presidents of both houses. At 11 AM, as the members bowed, he personally took his seat on the throne in the assembly hall. At this time, Prime Minister Hirota held the imperial rescript and approached the throne. The Emperor took it and read it. After the rescript was bestowed, President Koizumi received the imperial rescript and stepped down from the throne. The ceremony then ended, and the Emperor returned to the palace at 11:15 AM. (December 26, Domei)

(Tokyo) The plenary session of the House of Representatives on the day of the opening ceremony began at 11:30 AM. Vice-President Okada took the Speaker's chair and declared that a response to the imperial rescript must be drafted. He nominated Mr. Yoshiroku Nomura and eighteen others as members of the drafting committee. After introducing Mr. Ko Tanaka, who had just taken his seat, he adjourned for thirty-five minutes. During this time, the drafting committee drafted the response to the rescript. When the plenary session reconvened, the chairman reported, and the members stood up and passed the response. The session adjourned at 12:30 PM. (December 26, Domei)

(Tokyo) The response to the imperial rescript in the House of Representatives is as follows: "We, the Vice-President of the House of Representatives, Okada Tadahiko, respectfully and humbly report that we are deeply grateful for the honor of Your Majesty's personal attendance at the grand opening ceremony of the 70th session of the Imperial Diet and the bestowal of the gracious imperial rescript. We will carefully deliberate and fulfill our duty of cooperation, hoping to answer Your Majesty's will and fulfill the trust of the people." (December 26, Domei)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Finance's announced policy for budget compilation is as follows: "In order to respond to the current domestic and international situation in Japan, promote the country's fortune, and stabilize the people's lives, it is necessary to study many important facilities. Therefore, from 1937 onwards, the government will focus on strengthening national defense, reforming and improving education, improving the central and local tax systems, stabilizing the people's lives, promoting industry, expanding trade, establishing important policies towards Manchuria, and improving the administrative structure. These will be established as national policies, and their realization will be ensured. Therefore, when compiling the budget for 1937, the necessary expenses must be concentrated on the execution of important military and national policies. At the same time, efforts must be made to increase ordinary revenue in order to consolidate the foundation of finances. This is the policy adopted for this budget compilation." (December 26, Domei)

Japan Convenes Extraordinary Cabinet Meeting to Discuss Policies Towards China, Russia, and the Diet

(Tokyo) To deliberate and decide on important political affairs within the year and policies towards the Diet, an extraordinary cabinet meeting was held at the Prime Minister's official residence on the afternoon of the 26th. Prime Minister Hirota and other cabinet members attended. After deliberating and deciding on important political affairs within the year, Foreign Minister Arita reported on the temporary agreement on the Japan-Soviet fisheries treaty and the recent situation in China. He explained in detail the future trends of the Chinese political situation after Chiang Kai-shek's escape from Xi'an and discussed countermeasures. At the same time, they consulted on policies to deal with the Diet after its reopening on the 21st of next spring. (26th Kyodo News)

Prince Chichibu of Japan Decides to Visit England to Celebrate the Coronation and Tour Europe

(Tokyo) The Ministry of the Imperial Household announced that the British Emperor and Empress have set the coronation ceremony for May 12th next year. The Japanese Emperor is sending Prince Yasuhito to England to offer congratulations. The Princess will also accompany him. The two Highnesses are scheduled to depart from Yokohama in mid-March next spring aboard the Heian Maru, travel through Canada, and then take the British Queen Mary from New York to England, arriving around the 24th or 25th. After the coronation ceremony, they will tour various parts of Europe and return to Japan in the early spring of the following year. Chief Aide-de-Camp Matsudaira, Aide-de-Camp to Prince Chichibu Maeda, Military Attache Honma, Major General Niimi of the General Staff Headquarters, Rear Admiral Tomii of the Naval General Staff, and Councilor Yoshikawa of the British Embassy will be appointed within days. (26th Kyodo News)

Political Tide in Cuba

Havana, Cuba After former President Gomez was removed from office by a special tribunal of the Senate, Vice President Laredo Bru legally succeeded him. Political figures have recently stated that Army Chief of Staff Colonel Batista may force Laredo Bru to resign in the coming week. (25th Havas News)

Havana, Cuba The rumor that Army Chief of Staff Colonel Batista will force the new President Laredo Bru to resign has been denied by those around the Colonel. However, the majority of members of Congress still say a political storm is about to break out, and Cuba will soon establish a military dictatorship. According to the constitution, if the new president does resign, then the Prime Minister, General Montalvo, a confidant of Colonel Batista, will succeed as president. Political figures say that when former President Gomez left office, he issued a declaration accusing Colonel Batista of harboring dictatorial ambitions, which he directly admitted. Colonel Batista will surely respond to this. Yesterday, it was heard that he had a two-hour meeting with the new President Laredo Bru, but the contents of the conversation were not disclosed. Famous American Reporter Brisbane Passes Away with an Annual Salary of $250,000

(New York) Hearst newspaper reporter Brisbane passed away here at 5:30 this morning due to heart disease. Brisbane was involved in the newspaper business for 53 years. (25th National News)

(New York) Famous American journalist Arthur Brisbane died here today at the age of 72. Brisbane received an annual salary of $250,000 from the Hearst newspapers, and his writings were read by three to four million people. He opened a column called "Today" in two hundred newspapers, commenting on current events with a short and witty style. The writing was simple but flavorful, and it was published daily without interruption, making newspaper readers addicted to it. He also opened a column called "This Week" in 1,200 weekly magazines, chatting with rural people. Each Hearst weekly used large fonts to publish his full-page criticisms. Although unsigned, readers knew it was written by Brisbane. Brisbane was good at describing details to move the majority of readers. For example, on Washington's birthday, he discussed the size of the first president's feet, which was interesting and made readers reluctant to put it down. Brisbane returned to the country after studying in France and Germany for five years and served at the New York Sun. He was only 19 years old at the time. He later served as the chief editor of the New York World for seven years. In 1897, the circulation of the New York Evening Journal was only 40,000 copies, and it was on the verge of collapse. Brisbane was confident that he could increase the newspaper's circulation and save it, so he gave up his annual salary of $15,000 from the World and took the job at the Evening Journal with an annual salary of $7,500 to try his hand. Brisbane joined the Evening Journal in less than four months, and the circulation increased sharply because the editorials he wrote attracted readers. His contract with Hearst stipulated that his salary would increase according to the increase in the newspaper's circulation, so Brisbane's annual salary increased greatly, and he gained both fame and fortune. Brisbane had a very quick mind. He could dictate 1,200 to 1,500 words in 30 minutes. Brisbane set up an office in New York. When he crossed the Hudson River to return home every day, he always took a secretary with him and revised his articles on the ferry. Once, because he wanted to travel, he drafted 39 editorials in three hours so that the Evening Journal could use them before he returned. When Brisbane traveled, whether by boat or car, he always took a secretary and a typewriter. Even in the car, he dictated the text, and his secretary recorded it on the typewriter. On the train, he often used the sleeping car as an office. The Pullman train company always prepared the latest newspapers published in the area Brisbane passed through at the station and gave them to him when he arrived for him to use as source material. (25th Reuters News)

Japan Controls Military Industrial Production Expansion of Private Military Industry, Improvement of Production Each Factory Subject to Guidance and Supervision by the Military Department Naval and Army Arsenal Workers Reach 100,000

Tokyo Special Dispatch, The most noteworthy facility in Japan currently, which our country's citizens should pay attention to, is its control of military industrial production. This year's military budget is about 1.4 billion yuan, an increase of 340 million yuan compared to this year. The Army's six-year, 3.2 billion plan, (starting next year) and the Navy Department's third supplementary plan, show the new trend of Japan's expanding military spending. Therefore, military industrial production is also expanding accordingly. In Japan's military industrial production, state-owned enterprises account for a minority, and most rely on private industry. The details are as follows:

Private Industry

According to the Army Ministry's investigation, from Showa 6 (1931) to Showa 10, the total amount of military supplies expenses for these five years was 1.066 billion yuan, of which 785 million yuan was invested in private industry. In Showa 10, 68% of the Navy's military supplies were supplied by private industry. From this, we can see the relationship between private industry and military industrial production. After the expansion of military spending, it is absolutely necessary to strengthen the control of private military industry, such as expanding the capacity of private military industry, preventing price increases, suppressing high interest rates, controlling the connection between large capital industries and small and medium-sized industries, improving production technology and equipment, protecting secrets, and speeding up wartime merit awarding. All these issues are very necessary for controlling private military industrial production. The Japanese military is currently carefully considering strengthening military industrial production.

Current Control Situation

Japan's policy of controlling military industrial production has long existed. The Military Industry Mobilization Law formulated in Taisho 7 was the earliest control law. This was the result of the direct stimulation of the World War and the birth of the Soviet Union. However, it was only a law, and the enforcement regulations and implementation details were never announced. Although the Military Industry Control Law has not been implemented, there has been control in fact. (1) The Petroleum Industry Law forces petroleum companies to have oil storage obligations to protect domestic oil refining industry as its policy. (2) The Automobile Industry Law aims to develop domestic automobiles. These two laws both contain the meaning of business license control. At the same time, the government uses its power to strongly intervene in business plans to achieve the effect of control. On the surface, it is an ordinary economic control, but in fact, it mainly focuses on strengthening direct military industrial production. The currently proposed electricity control problem has gained strong support from the military because it indirectly contains the meaning of controlling military industrial production. In order to adapt to the expanding naval budget, the Ministry of Communications actively controls the shipbuilding industry and is currently reforming the Shipbuilding Industry Law. As for those that achieve control effectiveness without according to laws, on the Army's side, there are Japan Steel Works, Oshima Steel Works, Tengcang Factory, Sumitomo Copper Rolling, Japan Musical Instruments, Automobile Manufacturing, Nanbu Arsenal, Ishikawa Island Aircraft, Japan Vehicle, Automobile Industry, Hitachi Manufacturing, Domestic Industry, etc. On the Navy's side, there are Japan Battery, Mitsubishi Electric, Fujinagata Shipbuilding, Showa Production, Ishikawa Island Shipbuilding, Osaka Iron Works, Kawanishi Aircraft, Japan Wool Textile, Japan Fireworks, Japan Electric Industry, Teikoku Hemp Manufacturing, Japan Seiko, Kobukuro Workshop, Aichi Clock, etc. For both the Army and Navy, there are Mitsubishi Heavy Industries, Tokyo Instruments, Nippon Kogaku, Tokyo Gas Electric Industry, Kawasaki Shipbuilding, Nakajima Aircraft, Dangshi Electric, etc. Each factory is subject to the military's control, has the obligation to strictly maintain secrecy, and is subject to strict intervention and supervision regarding equipment capacity and the quality of manufactured goods.

Future Trends

In Showa 7, the Japanese Army Arsenal had 13,000 workers, and the Navy Arsenal had 38,000. Currently, the Army's ordinary workers and temporary workers have reached 32,000, and the Navy has expanded to 79,000, totaling 100,000. Although Japan's state-owned military industry is large-scale, it still cannot complete the task of expanding military spending next year. In the future, it will strive to guide the expansion of private productivity and strive to study how peacetime industrial production equipment can be converted into wartime military industrial factories. This point is similar to the situation in Germany on the eve of the European War, which is very noteworthy. (20th)

Xiamen Customs Cracks Down on Taiwanese Sailing Vessels Returning Home Strictly Preventing Smuggling and Importation of Contraband Goods Guangdong and Hong Kong Will Jointly Fight Smuggling

Xiamen Correspondence Smuggling into Fujian Province is mostly done by sailing vessels from Taiwan, which unload goods at various coastal ports in Quanzhou and Zhangzhou. Taiwan is separated from the southern Fujian coast by a strait, and the narrowest point is only 70 miles, which can be reached by sailing. However, if they can break through the patrol line of the customs inspection ships and reach the coast of Fujian Province, they can unload smuggled goods without hindrance. Therefore, the Xiamen Customs is extremely strict in inspecting civilian ships. On the 23rd of this month, a notice was issued, which stated, "It has been found that civilian ships returning to China from Taiwan must report to the Daguan Yinao Branch or Dongshan Branch for verification in accordance with the current regulations. Now, in order to facilitate the navigation of civilian ships from Taiwan to northern Fujian and the coastal areas of Zhejiang, it is stipulated that from January 1, 1937, all civilian ships that clear customs to any place and sail to places north of Beijiao in Fujian Province may directly sail to the Dongchong Branch of the Fuhai Customs (Sandu Ao) for verification. However, before leaving Taiwan, the civilian ship must first submit to the Chinese Consul-General in Taipei to stamp the ship's registration book. If the civilian ship does not have the registration book stamped by the Chinese Consul in Taipei and directly sails to the Dongchong Branch for verification, it will be considered smuggling, and the shipowner or captain will be punished in accordance with the revised regulations on the management of navigation and shipping of civilian ships by the customs. As for civilian ships clearing customs in Taiwan and sailing to places south of Jiaobei, they must still follow the current regulations and report to the Guanyin Ao Branch or Dongshan Branch for verification."

It is also heard that smugglers have recently secretly established smuggling cooperatives in various parts of Fujian and Guangdong to contact each other. Currently, many private merchants carry goods on each ship exporting from Hong Kong and smuggle them ashore in Shantou, Xiamen, or Fuzhou to evade taxes. There are countless tricks, and it is not easy to crack down on them. According to Xiamen Customs, the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance has not only ordered the Shantou, Xiamen, and Fuzhou customs to crack down on smuggling, but has also negotiated with the Hong Kong government on joint smuggling prevention measures. The Hong Kong government has agreed to strictly inspect smuggling from Hong Kong, which should make smugglers restrain themselves. (December 25th)

Rampant Bandits in the Suburbs of Guangzhou Bridges on the Luogangdong Highway Burned Down Sugar Cane Field in Chebei Sugar Factory Looted

Guangzhou Correspondence, In recent years, various parts of Guangdong Province have seen increasing rural bankruptcies and unemployment. Desperate and strong people who lack food and clothing are forced to take risks. In addition, the weather is cold at the end of the year, and unruly people are even more rampant. Robbery cases in villages and towns are frequent. The previous week, an incident was discovered in Luogangdong, a northeast suburb, where bandits burned down bridges on the Luogang highway. Luogangdong is only a dozen miles away from Guangzhou, and there is a lot of car and truck traffic every day. Luogangdong is one of the famous scenic spots in the suburbs. There is the Luofeng Temple there, and in winter, the plum trees bloom, and the color of the plum blossoms can be seen within 20 miles. Ladies and gentlemen who踏雪寻梅 leave many footprints. In summer, it is famous for producing fragrant lychees. A few years ago, the authorities designated several villages in the area as pilot areas for compulsory education and established compulsory primary schools. There is also a vegetable exhibition and the awarding of agricultural production certificates every year, so Luogangdong has gradually become a prosperous area. Bandits take advantage of this to covet the merchants and passengers who come and go, destroying bridges to rob vehicles. Fortunately, it was discovered early. The authorities have ordered the Panyu County government to instruct local gentry to investigate the bandits and strictly protect travelers. In addition, the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway is not far from the east of the city, and there is a station called Chebei, which is adjacent to Luogangdong. In the Yonghewei Village of Chebei near the station, there is a sugar cane field of the provincial sugar factory. There are employees inside who work every day and live in peace with each other. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 a.m. on the 19th, many bandits suddenly rushed into the factory, threatened the employees with guns and prohibited them from shouting. At the same time, several bandits looted all the silver, clothing, and bedding stored in the field. The employees then reported the case to the nearby Chebei Commune and the Dongpu Police Branch and reported the robbery to the provincial sugar factory, requesting that the local authorities be instructed to arrest the bandits and investigate the case. In addition to ordering the Panyu County government to investigate the case, the authorities have been strictly guarding against traffic in the near suburbs of the city and the city itself in recent days. Yesterday, military police were sent out to set up temporary inspection posts in the suburbs. After dark, they strictly inspected cars entering and leaving the urban area to prevent bandits from mixing in. These inspection stations are located at Shipai in Yijiao, the intersection of the Xizhai Civil Aviation Airport Road, the Liuhua Bridge outside the Dabeimen, the Gangxin Road intersection in Henan, and Shahe in the east suburbs. Each station is permanently guarded by military police. It is temporarily stipulated that privately owned cars and military vehicles within No. 3000 are exempt from inspection, but they must also pass slowly. Business vehicles and long-distance vehicles above No. 3001 should stop for inspection before passing through the station. Wooden posts are also erected on both sides of the road near the inspection post, and iron cables are hung from the wooden posts after dark, with red lights hung in the center of the iron cables, so that vehicles must stop as soon as they arrive and wait for inspection. However, all kinds of vehicles must stop for inspection at night. (December 24th)

Former Capital Relics Arrangement Committee Sixth Meeting - Planned Second Phase of Arrangement Project -

Beijing News: The first phase of the Former Capital Relics Arrangement Committee's project was completed in September of this year. To ensure the project's careful execution, the committee specially requested approval from the Executive Yuan and sent letters to relevant agencies inside and outside Beijing, requesting each to send representatives to Ping (Beiping) before October 1st to jointly inspect and accept the project. A total of twenty-five ancient architectural projects, including the Temple of Heaven's Circular Mound Altar, and ten road projects, including Xizhi Qinglong Road, were inspected and accepted. All were found to be solid, beautiful, clean, and have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for record. The second phase of the arrangement project has also been jointly investigated and planned by representatives of various project inspection teams. From the ancient buildings that were not repaired in the first phase, those that must be repaired in advance, those that are of greater historical and cultural significance, or those that are about to collapse due to their appearance, will be selected for priority arrangement. It is planned to include seventeen construction projects such as the Biyun Temple in the Western Hills, the Cenotaph of Sun Yat-sen, the Confucius Temple, and the Five Pagoda Temple, as well as the road project from Xisi Archway to Xizhimen. The arrangement method focuses on solidity and durability, and those related to appearance will also be appropriately decorated to achieve beauty. Currently, the second-phase project plan and the required funding have been compiled by the committee's Implementation Affairs Office. On the afternoon of the 16th of this month at 2:00 PM, the sixth meeting will be held in the conference hall of the Ministry of Interior to discuss the progress. Chairman Tao Lujian of the committee has telegraphed and approved requests to relevant agencies and the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee to send designated representatives to attend. It is reported that the important agenda items for this meeting are to discuss the scope and funding of the second phase of the arrangement project, as well as to submit a proposal to the Executive Yuan to continue handling the various suggested projects that could not be fully included in the second phase of the arrangement, and to revise the organizational rules of the Implementation Affairs Office.

Police Salaries Must Not Be Used for Other Purposes

The Administrative Commissioner's Office recently stated that the treatment of police officers is very poor, and the police salaries they are entitled to should be paid monthly. However, it has recently been found that the public security bureaus of various counties often divert police salary funds for other purposes. Continuing this practice is not a way to show compassion. Yesterday, a special order was issued to all counties, stipulating that police salary funds shall not be diverted for other expenses without authorization in the future, in order to clear accounts and maintain the use of police funds.

Since the beginning of winter in this county, it has not been severely cold. After a sudden shift to extreme cold following northwest winds, water has been freezing since the 23rd. Rivers and ports have also begun to freeze. The thermometer has dropped to 26 degrees Fahrenheit. One male beggar, in his forties, has already frozen to death in the eastern countryside.

All important transportation locations, whether day or night, must be strictly guarded. The county government has also issued a notice prohibiting rumors. Following Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's safe return to Nanjing after a perilous experience, the entire nation rejoiced. Yesterday, all sectors of the city celebrated by displaying flags, various organizations and groups sent congratulatory telegrams, schools held grand rallies to celebrate Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's safe escape from danger, and stock market prices uniformly surged. City Decorated with Flags

Upon learning that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who had been in distress for two weeks, had safely escaped danger, passed through Luoyang, and returned to Nanjing, the people of Shanghai were overjoyed. The previous evening, in both the Chinese and foreign concession areas, firecrackers were set off along the streets, their sound reverberating through the sky, continuing all night. Public Bonds Rise

Due to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's safe escape from danger, the morale of the people in Shanghai's stock, flour, yarn, miscellaneous grains, and other exchanges was greatly boosted, and they were exceptionally excited. Yesterday morning, when the first round of trading for various public bonds on the stock exchange opened, they all rose across the board. The price of the Unified Public Bond Series E was 62 yuan and 6 jiao, up 1 yuan and 4 jiao and a half. Series D was 64 yuan, up 1 yuan and 3 jiao. Series C was 62 yuan and 3 jiao, up 1 yuan and 2 jiao. Series B was 65 yuan and 4 jiao and a half, up 1 yuan and 3 jiao and a half. Series A was 73 yuan and 3 jiao and a half, up 1 yuan. Prices remained firm in the second round of trading. The third and fourth rounds of trading in the afternoon also remained stable. Other trading markets, such as flour, yarn, and miscellaneous grains, also reported uniform price increases.

Celebrating Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing, Citizens' Rally to be Held Tomorrow, At 2 PM at the Public Sports Ground on Dajilu Road, Preparatory Meeting to be Held at 10 AM this Morning to Discuss Measures

In order to prepare for celebrating Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's safe return to Nanjing, the Shanghai Municipal Party Branch yesterday invited representatives from Party and government agencies and various organizations to discuss measures for implementation. It was decided to convene a "Shanghai Citizens' Rally to Celebrate Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing," and after the meeting, a parade will be organized to express congratulations. The measures are recorded as follows:

Rally Measures (1) The name is designated as the Shanghai Citizens' Rally to Celebrate Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing. (2) The date is set for 2:00 PM on the 28th of this month (tomorrow). (3) The location is the Public Sports Ground in Nanshi.

Parade Order The order of the parade is as follows: police patrol vehicles, police band, police force, students and Boy Scouts, trained citizens, workers' organizations, security teams, other community organizations and citizens, and members of the defense corps. (2) Parade route: Starting from the northwest corner gate of the venue, via Fangxie Road, heading north, turning at Laoximen, heading south, walking along Zhonghua Road, passing Xiaoximen, Dananmen, Xiaonanmen, Dadongmen, to Xiaodongmen, walking along Fangbang Road, to Fangbang Bridge, heading north, walking along Minguo Road, passing Xiaobeimen, Dongxin Bridge, Kaobeimen, Xinkaihe, Xiaodongmen, to Dadongmen, walking along Zhaojia Road, exiting Laoximen, to Heping Road, where the parade will disband.

Other Districts As for Jiangwan, Wusong, Pudong, and other districts, due to the long distance, the party branches and military and political authorities in each district will hold separate celebration rallies in their respective districts on the same day. The measures may be based on the above measures and may be adjusted according to local conditions.

Preparatory Meeting The Municipal Party Branch has also scheduled a preparatory meeting for 10:00 AM today in the conference room of the branch on Fenglinqiao Road, inviting representatives from various agencies and organizations to discuss detailed measures for the citizens' celebration rally. It is heard that the invited agencies and organizations include: (1) the Municipal Government, (2) the Garrison Headquarters, (3) the Public Security Bureau, (4) the Social Affairs Bureau, (5) the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, (6) the General Labor Union, (7) the Education Association, (8) the Municipal Farmers' Association, (9) the Defense Committee, (10) the Civil Training Office, (11) party branches of various districts, (12) the Security General Corps Headquarters, (13) the Special Party Branch of the Security General Corps Headquarters, (14) the Seamen's Special Party Branch, (15) the Two Railways Special Party Branch, (16) the Lawyers' Association, (17) the Accountants' Association, (18) the Red Cross Society, (19) the Journalists' Association, and (20) the Citizens' Associations of the Two Special Districts.

Municipal Bureau of Public Works: Completion of Shanghai South No. 1 Warehouse, Leased to Minsheng Company for Exclusive Use for Ten Years, Tea Reception Yesterday to Invite People from All Walks of Life to Visit

The Public Works Bureau's Shanghai South No. 1 Warehouse, located in front of the Maojia Lane intersection on the outer road in Nanshi, is magnificent in construction and novel in equipment. Construction began in May of this year and was completed in seven months. It has been leased to Minsheng Industrial Company for exclusive use for ten years. A completion ceremony was held yesterday, inviting people from all walks of life to visit. Director Xu Peihuang of the bureau reported on the construction process. The details are as follows:

Tea Reception: The municipal warehouse is a five-story long building, horizontally erected in front of the Nanshi Outer Road, behind Pier No. 11 on the Pujiang Riverside Road. The entire building is white with steel windows, neat and magnificent, making it a major building in Shanghai South. Yesterday, a completion ceremony was held. More than a hundred people from all walks of life were invited to visit, including Yu Qiaqing, Gu Xinyi, Lin Jinyu, Zhang Shulin, and Tan Boying. They were greeted by staff and toured the rooms. Tea and refreshments were served on the third floor. During the reception, Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Works Bureau, reported on the construction of the warehouse. This was followed by a speech by Yu Qiaqing, a senior figure in the shipping industry, who stated that he was delighted that the municipal authorities and shipping merchants had cooperated to complete this new type of warehouse. He recalled that when Zhang Yuejun was in charge of Shanghai, he had offered advice to have the city government organize and sub-lease the piers of the Shiliupu to various shipping companies, which was adopted. The situation is now well-organized. This time, Minsheng Industrial Company and the municipal government have completed the construction of the warehouse, and the facilities are even more perfect. He hoped that other companies could also cooperate in construction to facilitate shipping and develop industry and commerce. Next, Zhang Shulin, Manager of Minsheng Industrial Company, gave a speech. He said that Minsheng Company has a relatively short history, having only established a branch in Shanghai for five years. Previously, the lack of a pier caused inconvenience for both passengers and cargo. A few years ago, the Public Works Bureau approved the lease of Piers No. 11 and 12. Now, the Public Works Bureau has built a new warehouse, leased to the company for exclusive use for ten years, with perfect facilities, and the company will work harder to provide services. It is said that the construction cost of the warehouse was about 210,000 yuan, and it will be managed by the Public Works Bureau Pier Warehouse Management Committee and will be put into use on New Year's Day next year.

Warehouse Facilities: The warehouse base covers an area of 1.588 acres, forming a narrow and long shape. The length from north to south is 90.49 meters (296 feet 10 inches), the width at the north end is 8.5 meters (28 feet), and the width at the south end is 16.95 meters (55 feet 7 inches). The area is 1,078 square meters (11,600 square feet). The internal layout of the first floor includes the customs office, private goods storage room, inspection room, Minsheng Company manager's office, office reception room, warehouse, management room, washroom, crane room, elevator room, and storage room. The second, third, fourth, and fifth floors are all storage rooms. The total net storage area inside the warehouse is 3,927.5 square meters (42,260 square feet), and the net open-air storage area on the roof is 870 square meters (9,370 square feet). Therefore, the storage capacity of the municipal warehouse is more than 5,000 tons. The height of the building, from the first floor to the roof, is 18.6 meters (61 feet). The first floor is 0.61 meters (2 feet) above the road surface, so that goods inside will not be wet when the tide rises. The project and materials strive for solidity. All columns, beams, foundations, roofs, stairs, and floor slabs are made of steel and concrete to ensure durability and fire resistance. The foundation piles are all made of round wooden piles of 18.29 meters (60 feet) and 21.34 meters (70 feet) in length. The warehouse site was formed by filling with soil by the Dredging Bureau, and it has only been twenty years. The soil is loose and cannot bear heavy loads, so it is necessary to drive long piles to achieve solidity. In addition, underground beams are built on top of the wooden piles to quickly connect all the piles. In this way, even if the house subsides, it will be a complete and even drop, without unevenness or cracks. Internal equipment pays the most attention to facilitating the loading and unloading of goods and preventing fires. There are three types of equipment to facilitate the loading and unloading of goods: one is an escalator, with a gentle slope for easy walking; the second is an elevator, with two elevators, each with a load capacity of 1.996 kilograms (2 tons, i.e., 4,400 pounds) and a speed of 35 meters per minute; the third is a unloading machine, also known as a crane, with two cranes installed on the fifth floor for unloading. The load capacity is 762 kilograms (3/4 ton, i.e., 1,680 pounds). All operations are done manually. The manufacturing cost is low, and its application in domestic warehouses is still a pioneering effort. The crane room is equipped with sliding doors, and cargo trucks can drive in from the road and load and unload goods indoors, so even on rainy days, the goods will not be wet. As for fire prevention design, it is even more meticulous. The warehouse building frame is made of steel and concrete, and the brick walls are covered with cement and yellow sand, so there is no risk of fire. In the escalator office, all doorways connecting to the storage area are equipped with fire doors. In case of an accident, the fire doors can close automatically to prevent the spread of fire. There are also five fire escape ladders around the building, and each floor is equipped with a fire platform so that firefighters can climb onto the platform to rescue in case of a fire. In addition, there are two types of fire fighting equipment: one is a fire hydrant system, with one fire hydrant in each storage area, equipped with various accessories such as fire hoses. In case of a fire, the fire hose is connected to the hydrant, and water can be released for rescue. The second is an automatic fire extinguisher, installed under the floor slabs of each floor. Every three square meters is equipped with a fire extinguisher, shaped like a faucet, with the opening sealed with a fuse. Water will not overflow. If a fire occurs and the temperature in the room rises to 58 degrees Celsius, the fuse will melt, and water will spray outwards to extinguish the fire, which is very effective. For fire fighting water, two water tanks are placed on the roof in case the tap water supply is insufficient or the pressure is too low.

Zou Lu Went to Beijing Yesterday Morning to Meet with Central Authorities and Chiang

Central Committee member Zou Lu arrived in Shanghai from Guangdong by boat on the 25th and stayed at the Cangzhou Hotel. He visited Yang Shukan, Xu Chongzhi, Cai Yuanpei, and Qin Zhen, Vice President of the Judicial Yuan, who were in Shanghai. Zou and his wife, son, Xie Mingzhang, Wu Zhimei, and others took the 8:00 AM express train to Beijing yesterday morning to meet with key members of the central government and await a meeting with Chairman Chiang.

Municipal Party Headquarters: Rectifying District Branches, Registering and Completing Procedures on Time, Reorganizing District Branches

The Municipal Party Headquarters of this city, in order to promote the work of the district branches, has specially drafted rectification measures and issued a notice for re-registration. The original text is recorded as follows: "For the purpose of notifying matters, this committee has specially drafted preliminary measures for rectifying the leaders of the district branches in order to improve the organization of the district branches and promote the work of the district branches. The measures have been submitted to the Central Committee for approval and record. According to these measures, all district branches in this city must be reorganized, and all party members must re-register with the district party headquarters. This is a special notice. All party members and probationary party members residing in this city, regardless of whether they have participated in a district branch, must bring their party card and a 2.5-inch half-length photo to the following locations on January 9th and 10th of the 26th year, from 9:00 AM to 7:00 PM, to complete the registration and fill out the form, and wait to be assigned to the new district branch for work. Otherwise, they will be deemed to have lost their party membership in this city. Do not neglect this matter. This is the main point. This is a special notice. The locations for party members to register are: (1) District Party Headquarters in the city; (2) 2nd District Party Headquarters in the French Concession; (3) 3rd District Party Headquarters in the Tianhou Temple; (4) 4th District Party Headquarters in Hongkou; (5) 5th District Party Headquarters in Pudong; (6) 6th District Party Headquarters in Zhabei; (7) 7th District Party Headquarters in Jiangwan; (8) 8th District Party Headquarters in Wusong; (9) 9th District Party Headquarters in Longhua; (10) 10th District Party Headquarters in Beixinjing; (11) First Directly Affiliated District Party Headquarters of Jinan University in Zhenru."

For the Issue of Manufacturing and Selling Gas Masks: Unified Guidance Methods, Air Defense Association Creates Two Types of Registration Forms: Manufacturers and People Must First Fill Them Out Before Instructions Are Given

The Shanghai Air Defense Association, recently in view of the fact that there are many manufacturers in this city who independently manufacture and sell gas masks, and many civilians blindly prepare them, is concerned that merchants may only be interested in profits or lack skills, inevitably cutting corners and producing shoddy products, so that the products are not enough to defend against poison gas and are difficult to ensure safety, which is very dangerous. It is also worried that allowing civilians to buy them casually will easily fall into the hands of traitors, who will turn to help bandits, which is even more harmful. Therefore, the association has issued a public notice in newspapers, calling on the people to pay attention and carefully select purchases to avoid wasting money and being deceived. On the other hand, it has also submitted a request to the highest military and political authorities for rapid control measures and the implementation of manufacturing and sales management to prevent abuses. It is said that after the news was revealed, manufacturers of gas masks and people concerned about gas prevention have flocked to the association to request instructions, and they are overwhelmed. Now, in order to seek a unified guidance method to facilitate both manufacturers and people, the association has now created a gas mask manufacturing registration form and a purchase registration form. Those who want to request instructions, such as manufacturers, must first fill out the manufacturing registration form, and people must first fill out the purchase registration form, then the association will give detailed instructions. It is also said that the forms can be obtained directly from the association or by enclosing postage.

After the death of National Government member Huang Fu, the remains were moved at noon yesterday at the China Funeral Home on Haig Road. Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Pan Gongzhan, Yang Hu, and Yu Hongjun served as the presidium. Zhou Yongneng read the memorial text, Yuan Liang reported on Huang Fu's life, and his family member Huang Yaonian expressed his gratitude.

Memorial Text of the Meeting

On December 26th, the 25th year of the Republic of China, the party, government, military, and police agencies of Shanghai, as well as various agencies, groups, and people from all walks of life, respectfully offer incense, flowers, and wine to the spirit of National Government Member Huang Yingbai, saying, Alas, recalling the past years, the country is in unprecedented difficulties. In the struggle to resist foreign aggression and revitalize the nation, you took the lead. In Zhejiang, you abandoned your pen and discussed military affairs with patriots. You secretly planned reforms and were determined to sacrifice. You first went to the East and joined the Tongmenghui with great enthusiasm. As a man of courage, you implemented your plans. In the autumn of the Xinhai Revolution, all sides were united in hatred. You and the Shanghai Governor had deep mutual understanding. You entered the command tent and took charge of the troops. You planned the advance and took charge of the strategy. You transported supplies and arms. In a few months, you recovered China. Whose merits can compare with yours? After the establishment of the Republic of China, you were humble and unpretentious. You took the lead in relinquishing your post, creating a new atmosphere. How could we have foreseen that great villains would rise up at that time, deceiving us with treachery? They harmed good people and trampled on justice. You and the Shanghai Governor resumed the righteous crusade. Heaven did not bless us, and the righteous banner suddenly fell. You traveled to the United States and Japan, determined to rebuild. The Anmin Society advocated, and the country's path shifted imperceptibly. The Southwest Protectorate was almost unsustainable. Your anger was aroused, and you quickly returned to your hometown. You supported the independence of Zhejiang Province. Before long, you raised the banner of righteousness. The country was pacified, and you did not claim credit for your achievements. You retired to Tianjin and devoted yourself to writing books. With foresight and prescience, you deeply pondered the lessons of the European War. You were determined to save the times and entered the government several times. Your grand plans and regulations are worthy of being passed down for thousands of years. The revolutionary army rose from the South. The righteous banner pointed to the hope of contact. You and Feng Yuxiang shared the same heart and mind. You secretly discussed the response to achieve penetration. The foundation in the North was thus successful. China was unified, and Nanjing was established as the capital. You continued your efforts and served as the mayor of Shanghai. You used people and administered the government with utmost impartiality. The scale and order became a national model. You then took charge of the altar, but a great disaster suddenly occurred. You painstakingly tried to salvage the situation, regardless of gains or losses. National opinions were divided. You lived in the mountains to express your ambition, practiced metaphysics, and did not forget national affairs. You taught and established societies, being impartial and not partisan. You led the wise and presided over the atmosphere. As the years became more treacherous, and strong enemies roamed, you accepted the order with a sigh and went north in a hurry. You resisted the enemy alone, relying only on sincerity. The northern border was thus safe, and the overall situation was stable. Matters were as tangled as silk, and your hard work was high. You made concessions in adversity, and ultimately became ill. Alas, my lord, you forgot yourself for the country, and did not refuse hard work and complaints. With iron shoulders, you unswervingly upheld righteousness. Alas, my lord, you are a hero of all ages. Those who come after will never forget your loyalty to the country. May you enjoy this offering.

Memorial Text of the National Government

Chairman Lin of the National Government specially sent Mayor Wu to offer a memorial text, saying, On December 26th, the 25th year of the Republic of China, Chairman Lin Sen of the National Government specially sent Mayor Wu Tiecheng of Shanghai to respectfully offer incense and pay tribute to the spirit of National Government Member Huang Yingbai, saying, Alas, the ocean tide is turbulent, and the country's path is difficult. Heaven does not pity us and has taken away our wise man. It is difficult to find talents to save the world, a common lament of ancient and modern times. The grand structure is being built, but the beam is suddenly lost. In your life, you were born in Zhejiang, endowed with intelligence. With ambitions like wind and clouds, and intelligence like ice and snow, you took the reins in Japan, with a high ambition for the universe. With the ability to adapt and store talent, you were endowed with both literary and military skills. You followed the Father of the Nation and allied overseas, uniting your comrades and following the principles. After the Xinhai Revolution, the Republic was established. You took charge of national plans and assisted in the new model. You took the lead in advocating disarmament, setting an example for the military. You soared high over thousands of miles in the South. Xiangcheng stole the country, and you went to the rescue with a crown. Riding through the ranks, you saw a line of life. You traveled far to search for political news, pondered the past, and revealed it to the people. To govern the country, talent is needed, and it is difficult to ensure impartiality. You rose again in the East Mountains to uphold the overall situation. You pushed your comrades forward with a sincere heart, moving eastwards towards the sea. You secretly supported the National Army and facilitated reunification. Without boasting or claiming credit, who could have known your deep plans? You took over the municipal government and later took charge of foreign affairs. Before your plans could be completed, your reputation was even more evident. You retired to an empty mountain, longing for national politics. You secretly discussed good plans, never forgetting your loyalty. In the 22nd year, the national crisis deepened. The bustling Yan City was filled with wind and cranes. You accepted the order and went north, feeling the difficulty. You made concessions in diplomacy. You were the only one who could be relied on. You weighed the situation and responded appropriately. You silently used your spirit to manage this crisis, hoping to plan for the future and care for the people. You had ways to heal the country, and your skills were hard-won. You did not claim credit for your achievements, and did not shirk responsibility for your faults. With sincerity for the country, you did not seek people's knowledge. In the stormy and dangerous boat, you supported it in the middle of the stream. Your heart and strength were exhausted, and your worries were different. You suffered from illness in Shanghai, and the days passed slowly. People in the central government praised you, and the public hoped to return. We hoped for your grand plans to bless our party and country. How could it be that you suddenly passed away and your spirit went to the stars? Your last words were earnest, and you were concerned about national affairs. You remained in our thoughts. The safety of East Asia was on your mind. Alas, my lord, why did you depart so quickly? Your loyalty and love can be made in the nine springs. There are classics for the funeral, and the central government praised you. The ceremony was a public burial, the light of Wu and Yue. It is not easy to pacify foreign and internal troubles. It is difficult to lose people in times of trouble, and the world is melancholy. Your merits are immortal, and your model still exists. We respectfully offer fragrant offerings and respectfully inform your spirit. May you enjoy this offering.

How could it be that you suddenly passed away in Shanghai? Your last words on your sickbed were concerned about national affairs. Your loyalty was unwavering. Even in death, you were still watching. The people shed tears, and the officials were sad. Your name will be passed down forever, and your achievements will be recorded. The rain in the borderland is bleak, and the north wind is cold. Inland River Steamboat Industry Association Holds General Meeting Yesterday, Elects Executive and Supervisory Committee Members to Raise Funds, Telegraphs Ministry of Communications to Implement Three Regulations

The Inland River Steamboat Industry Association of this city held its sixth general meeting yesterday. More than 40 people attended. Zhu Yakui from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhang Dafu from the Bureau of Social Affairs, and Sun Wuzhi from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended to guide the meeting. (2) Qingshou Shipping Bureau's application to withdraw from the association due to dissatisfaction with the handling of Dali Company's expansion of joint transportation cargo routes was resolved to advise the bureau to remain in the association. (3) The application of Bianli Shipping Company to withdraw from the association due to suspension of operations was resolved to approve. (4) The application to remove the Faji Ren Shipping Bureau due to its sale was resolved to approve. (6) The budget for last year and the budget for this year were resolved to pass. (6) It was resolved in principle to submit the industry regulations to the Bureau of Social Affairs for record, and to distribute them to members for comments within a limited time for separate discussion. (7) The fundraising plan was resolved to pass in principle and handed over to the Executive and Supervisory Committee for handling. The original text reads, To Minister Yu of the Ministry of Communications in Nanjing, We hereby respectfully submit that today the association held its sixth general meeting, and regarding the three regulations promulgated by your ministry for the reorganization of the private shipping industry, namely the Steamboat Industry Registration Regulations, the Steamboat Industry Supervision Regulations, and the Measures to Promote the Aviation Industry, we request that you order their implementation as soon as possible in order to achieve results. We hereby submit this telegram for your inspection, Shanghai Inland River Steamboat Industry Association, Sixth General Meeting, Presidium, Han Yimin, Cao Rongqing, Zhou Baozhi, bowing together.

Public Notices from the Social Affairs and Health Bureaus: Regulations for Establishing Factory Health Rooms - Stipulating that Factories Regularly Employing 300 or More Workers Must Comply with These Regulations and Establish Health Rooms

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, acting on instructions from the Feng City Government, forwarded the "Regulations for Establishing Health Rooms in Factories" promulgated by the Central Factory Inspection Bureau. Previously, it was jointly announced with the Health Bureau to inform the public, stipulating that all factories regularly employing 300 or more workers must comply with these regulations. The regulations are as follows: (1) Matters concerning medical and health affairs in factories shall be handled in accordance with these regulations, unless otherwise stipulated by law. (2) Matters to be handled by the medicine room stipulated in Article 17 of the Factory Implementation Regulations and the medical room stipulated in Article 70 of the Detailed Rules for Factory Safety and Health Inspection shall be handled by the factory health room. (3) The factory health room shall, under the direction of the factory owner, handle the following matters: 1. Research and improvement of workplace health technology; 2. Diagnosis, treatment, and first aid for worker injuries and illnesses; 3. Research and improvement of environmental sanitation; 4. Research and prevention of infectious and occupational diseases; 5. Guidance and training on worker health education; 6. Worker health care; 7. Procurement and management of medical supplies and equipment; 8. Worker injury and illness statistics; 9. Other matters related to factory health. (4) The factory health room shall, when handling the matters listed in the preceding article, comply with the relevant provisions of the Revised Factory Implementation Regulations and the Detailed Rules for Factory Safety and Health Inspection concerning factory health. (5) For the various items listed in Article 3 that are related to personnel, engineering, and general affairs, the factory health room shall handle them jointly with the relevant department heads. (6) If the factory health room is of a larger scale, it may be divided into the following groups for work convenience: 1. Health Affairs Group; 2. Treatment Group; 3. Pharmacy Group. (7) The number of personnel in the factory health room shall be determined according to the actual situation within the factory, but it must have at least one director who also serves as a physician, one nurse, one part-time pharmacist, and one health inspector. (8) The director of the factory health room shall be appointed from among those who are well-versed in hygiene and medical knowledge and experience. (9) The factory health room shall, to the extent possible, set up temporary sick rooms and isolation rooms. (10) The factory health room shall assign personnel to rotate on duty outside of working hours. (11) If workers and apprentices in the factory fall ill, they shall be diagnosed and treated at the factory during the prescribed hours, except for special emergencies where the doctor may make a house call. (12) The factory health room shall consider and formulate the following rules and post them in appropriate places: 1. Workplace Hygiene Rules; 2. Worker Diagnosis Rules; 3. Worker Dormitory Hygiene Rules; 4. Worker Dining Hall Hygiene Rules; 5. Worker Kitchen Hygiene Rules; 6. Worker Washroom and Bathroom Hygiene Rules; 7. Worker Toilet Hygiene Management Rules; 8. Worker Physical Examination and Defect Correction Rules; 9. Various Occupational Disease and Infectious Disease Prevention Rules; 10. Worker Temporary and Isolation Room Hospitalization Rules; 11. Other rules related to factory hygiene. (13) The factory health room shall compile the following statistics: Injury and illness statistics - Occupational disease statistics - Vaccination statistics - Mortality statistics - Health examination statistics - Injury and illness classification statistics - Infectious disease statistics - Environmental sanitation improvement statistics.

Car Donation Meeting - Meeting Procedures

The Chinese Red Cross Society, the China National Road Construction Association, and the Joint Disaster Relief Association of Charitable Organizations, in order to rescue wounded soldiers and women and children in distress at the front lines, specially launched a campaign to raise vehicles to be transported to the front lines to meet urgent needs. A meeting was convened a few days ago to discuss the implementation methods. A committee was established to oversee the project, consisting of nine members, with representatives from the three organizations and major foreign automobile merchants. The committee held its first meeting at the New Asia Hotel at 5:00 PM on the 22nd of this month. The attending committee members were Zhao Jinqing, Yan Fuqing, Qian Xinzhi (represented by Lou Zan), Lou Wangzuan, Crowe (Ford Motor Company), Freeman (China Motor Company, representative of Myers, Lachaia (General Motors Company), Smith (Marty Motor Company), Dai Youshan (Youfu Body Manufacturing Company), with Zhao Jinqing as Chairman and Wei Guoying as Secretary. The important matters resolved to be carried out included: (1) The goal for vehicle fundraising is temporarily set at 20 trucks, and the necessary funds will be raised by the three organizations. (2) The three organizations will jointly request the Ministry of Finance to waive import duties on these vehicles. (3) Regarding the method of purchasing vehicles, each foreign member will be responsible for planning, with the price based on the factory cost of the vehicle and a further reduction if possible. Committee member Dai will be responsible for body manufacturing, contacting various manufacturers, and also aiming to reduce the manufacturing cost to the cost price. The meeting adjourned at 8:00 PM.

Chen Ruiqi, President of the Hong Kong Daozi Research Society, recognizing the widespread suffering of compatriots in Suiyuan following the outbreak of bandit suppression warfare, generously donated HK$60,000 and dispatched cadres Chen Yaoxiong, Chen Mengyin, He Heming, Cheng Wanli, and others to form a disaster relief group.
