The majority of members and colleagues of the Shanghai Overseas Students Association in the UK were extremely excited by the news of the victory of the Suiyuan National Army. In order to encourage the soldiers at the front, the association specially entrusted the Bank of China to telegraph $50 in national currency to the Suiyuan Provincial Government yesterday for the purpose of rewarding the soldiers at the front. At the same time, a telegram was sent to General Fu Zuoyi, Chairman of the Suiyuan Provincial Government, to commend them. The original telegram reads: "(Omission above) The bandits and puppets invaded Suiyuan, thanks to your heroic battles, Bai Lingmiao was conquered in one fell swoop, and the Da Miao was pacified in the second. The righteous army is invincible wherever it points. From afar, we admire your bravery. We have arranged for the Bank of China to remit $50 in national currency to reward the soldiers at the front. We also hope that you will encourage the soldiers and continue to strive for complete success. The country is fortunate. Shanghai Overseas Students Association bows in respect."

Fudan Affiliated Middle School's Enthusiastic Support for Suiyuan

The Fudan University Affiliated Middle School's support movement for Suiyuan has been consistent from beginning to end. In addition to long-term food conservation by all students and the establishment of a savings box, it also promoted a frugal patriotic movement. It joined forces with the university department of the school to issue frugal gift certificates. Recently, the female students of the school launched a silk wadded vest aid movement for Suiyuan. Wang Jiaoying, Xu Li, Chen Yuling, Tan Zhonglan, and others donated $10 each to purchase a large quantity of silk wadding and blue cloth, and worked overnight to make silk wadded vests. In the past week, more than 100 pieces have been completed. Among the male students, Zhou Henggen donated the most, recognizing 12 pieces. It is said that they will be sent to the bandit suppression soldiers in Suiyuan soon. The savings box set up by the school is opened once a week, and the results are excellent. Yesterday, the former principal of the school, Mr. Li Denghui, returned to Shanghai from a trip to Sichuan. Student representatives Zhou Jiazhang, Chen Zhicheng, Zhang Yannian, Zhang Youhong, Xu Shuren, Yu Shixiang, Li Xianzheng, Yu Shuntai, Zha Dagang, Xu Yingrui, Li Shiying, Wei Houmei, and others went to Longmao Pier on Wuma Road to welcome him. On the way back, they voluntarily lined up and walked back to school from the Bund, donating all the saved fare to the savings box. Such patriotic spirit is rare.

China National Aviation Corporation - The Shanghai-Chengdu Route Remains Normal - Cause of the Fire on the Sichuan Plane - The Head Office Has Not Received a Detailed Report

The Douglas giant plane Sichuan, which flies on the Shanghai-Chengdu route for China National Aviation Corporation, caught fire at Chengdu Airport and was completely destroyed. The reporter learned from China National Aviation Corporation that all passengers and mail on the plane were unharmed, because the fire occurred while the plane was still at the airport. As for the cause of the fire, the head office authorities will make a public statement after receiving a detailed report. The route is still operating as usual, and another plane was dispatched from Chengdu on the morning of the 26th. The new planes that the company ordered from the United States are expected to arrive in Shanghai next spring due to the strike of American sailors.

Cen Chai Suffers from Coal Poisoning - On a Night When Her Husband Did Not Return - She Lost Her Life

Cen Chai, a woman from Shaoxing, was 21 years old. She lived with her husband, Cen Zenglai, at No. 11, Lane 557, Dongyouheng Road. It happened that her husband was not at home the night before. Because she was afraid of the cold, she lit a coal briquette stove in the bedroom for warmth and closed the windows tightly, causing coal poisoning. It was not until 7:00 AM the next morning, when her husband returned home, that he found her unconscious in bed. He rushed her to Shanghai Nursing Home for treatment, but she soon died. The hospital reported to the Jiuxing Road Police Station in charge, who sent investigators to investigate. The body was then taken to the Phelon Road Mortuary. Yesterday morning, Song Genshan, Prosecutor of the First Special Court, went to the mortuary and confirmed that the body belonged to Cen Chai, a female, and that she had died from coal gas poisoning. The body was released to her husband, Cen Zenglai, to be claimed for burial after he signed a statement.

Sampan Capsizes - Seven People Fall into the River and Are Rescued

Wang Baoyi, from Jiangbei, together with his sister-in-law, Mrs. Chen, and five children, Xingan and Xingming, recently arrived in Shanghai on the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tai Shun steamer. Yesterday morning at 2:30 AM, after the steamer docked at the Jinliyuan Wharf on the 16th Pier, Wang and others were greeted by his cousin Wang Baogui and friend Qian Yuansheng, and boarded Sampan No. 849 to cross to Yangjiadu in Pudong to return home. At this time, three garbage boats were rushing to dock. Because the sampan had not yet left the dock, it was violently rammed by Garbage Boat No. 30542 and capsized, and seven passengers, both adults and children, fell into the river at the same time. Fortunately, they were rescued separately by the French Concession Chinese police and the garbage boat crews. Because all seven people had swallowed a considerable amount of river water, they were rushed to Guangci Hospital on Jinshenfu Road for treatment, and fortunately, they were all safe. Later, Li Wenqi, a Chinese detective from the Customs Water Police Station, took Zhou Xuecai, the crew of the offending boat, along with the luggage of the seven people, to the police station for investigation.

Police Chief Receives Bribe and Is Sent for Investigation

Recently, there have been gambling incidents at the Longxing Secondhand Shop at No. 66 Linping Road, Zhabei. Police Chief Huang Yulin found out about this and privately went to collect a bribe of $6. Huang feared being reported and submitted the bribe to the station, reporting the incident and requesting handling. While the station was in the process of summoning him, Police Chief Huang suddenly deserted his post and fled, fearing punishment. His whereabouts are unknown. The station has submitted a request to the General Bureau to instruct police teams in various districts to investigate and arrest him. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, Police Chief Huang, knowing that it was difficult to escape, surrendered to the station. After interrogation, it was found that Wang Yousan, a police officer, was also involved, and he was detained. As the case involved public officials privately accepting bribes, the relevant documents were prepared and delivered to the Third Section of the General Bureau for investigation in the afternoon.

Customs Notice - Adding Light Piles to Ningbo Port - Vessels Sailing on the Shanghai-Ningbo Route Should Pay Attention

The Customs issued a notice yesterday stating that the waterways at Zhangjianqi and Meixu (belonging to Ningbo Port) under the jurisdiction of the Zhejiang Customs are difficult to navigate and light piles should be added immediately to facilitate navigation. As of the 20th of this month, one light pile has been erected at each of the above two locations, 35 feet high, made of wooden poles, with a black spherical marker on top, each with a non-rated red warning light. In addition to having been submitted to the Tax Commissioner for approval, this notice is hereby issued. The locations of the two light piles are listed below for the information of merchants. (1) Zhangjianqi pile, on the left bank of the waterway, is 299 degrees north of true north, and is 9.35 chains from Dongshan. (2) Meixu light pile, on the left bank of the river, is 284 degrees north of true north, and is 2.85 chains from the northeast corner of the white house on the right bank of the Meixu river. (3) Relevant maps are the Hydrographic Chart No. 501 of the Naval Department of the Republic of China.

Qiaqing Hospital Preparatory Committee - Decides on Architectural Design

The Architectural Design Committee of Qiaqing Hospital held a meeting at the Preparatory Office of the Hospital at No. 93 Guangdong Road the day before yesterday. The committee members present were Yan Fuqing, Li Dachao, Wang Xiaolai, Gu Yuqi, and Zhang Jiguang. The attending members were Mao Heyuan, Director-General, and Li Yang'an, Architect. Yan Fuqing was the Chairman, and Shen Wangyun was the Secretary. The resolved matters are recorded below: (1) Regarding the decision on the architectural design, it was resolved that the drawings prepared by Architect Li Yang'an be approved with modifications, and the roof should be changed to a flat roof. (2) Regarding the decision on the construction site, it was resolved that the Municipal Works Bureau be requested to designate the routes of Guoping North Road and Zhengning Road according to the current drawings, preferably moving the route of Guoping North Road to the east and the route of Zhengning Road to the south. (3) Regarding the construction and equipment budget, it was resolved that the construction cost, including the water heating system, should be $60,000 in national currency, the equipment cost should be $20,000, and the foundation fund should be $20,000. (4) Regarding the scheduled date for bidding, it was resolved that Architect Li be requested to prepare formal drawings and an estimate to be submitted to the meeting before January 15th, for further review. (5) Regarding the scheduled date for commencement of construction, it was resolved that the formal drawings and estimate should be submitted to the Preparatory Committee on January 15th for a decision.

National Goods Joint Venture Company - All Sectors Enthusiastically Subscribe to Shares - The Goal of $1 Million Can Be Achieved - Shanghai Has the Most Participants

The China National Goods Joint Venture Company, initiated by the General Committee of the National Economic Construction Movement, has been actively recruiting shareholders since inviting leaders from all sectors across the country to form a preparatory committee and holding a preparatory meeting in Beijing, where the preparatory office was formally established. The articles of association, prospectus, share subscription form, and other documents were sent to various factories, companies, banks, and money shops for recruitment. According to a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, the total capital stock of the company is temporarily set at $2 million in legal tender, divided into 4,000 shares, each share being $500. The capital is raised in two phases. In the first phase, 2,000 shares are raised, with the government subscribing to one-third and national goods factories and companies subscribing to two-thirds. All shares must be paid in full before the company is established, but individuals are not allowed to subscribe in their own names. If national goods factories and companies are willing to subscribe to more shares than the aforementioned quota, a portion of the government shares may be allocated to allow commercial shares to be subscribed. After the company is established, if newly established national goods factories and companies and consumer cooperatives in various regions that have not joined wish to subscribe to shares, a portion may also be transferred from the government shares. The second phase of capital, $1 million, will be raised after the company has been established for one year, as determined by the board of directors. Therefore, national goods companies, factories, consumer cooperatives, and others in various regions are enthusiastically subscribing to shares, especially in Shanghai. It is expected that the goal of $1 million will be reached soon, and a second preparatory meeting will be scheduled to discuss further preparatory matters.

Yesterday, Shanghai District Court Strictly Interrogated the Ye Fu Kang Case; Lawyers Gu Ao and Gu Ji Rong Appeared in Court to Present Arguments; Repeatedly Questioned the Revocation of the Complaint by Wang Han Qing; Ye Stated That There Was No Such Person as Li Sun Min, Requesting Confrontation; the Court Ordered a Change of Date to Re-examine When Wang Han Qing Arrives in Court

Former Judge of the Shanghai District Court, now the owner of a small Lu Song hat shop, lawyer Ye Fu Kang, was accused by Wang Han Qing, a Henan native who previously worked as a detective in the Hankou Public Security Bureau, in a complaint to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, of embezzling a large sum of money under the pretext of defending a case. The Ministry ordered the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor Tang to prosecute Ye Fu Kang, and a public prosecution was initiated. However, before the public trial, Wang Han Qing suddenly hired lawyer Gu Ji Rong to draft a statement requesting revocation and confessing to making false accusations. Wang himself fled to another port and never appeared in court. The court noted that Ye Fu Kang had twice, in 1933 and last year, reached settlements through lawyers Gu Ao, Zha Ruwei, Cai Ding, Shen Zengkuan, and others. According to Ye, he only received public funds of 4,000 yuan, while according to Gu Ao, the two settlements involved Ye Fu Kang returning as much as 6,300 yuan. In the previous summons of witness Hu Jin Kun, it was also stated that after this lawsuit, lawyer Gu Ao also brought a receipt for Ye Fu Kang's 20,000 yuan bail to the Great British Apartments to settle with Wang Han Qing, saying he was willing to pay 10,000 yuan to settle the matter. Judge Lu Hongyi of the court then ordered a cross-examination at 10:00 AM yesterday. Only Gu Ao and Gu Ji Rong arrived. The questioning officer asked Gu Ao, who admitted to the previous settlement but denied this one, also stating that he had never been to the Great British Apartments. He said that Wang Han Qing and others wanted 10,000 yuan, and when Ye Fu Kang questioned them after this lawsuit, he and lawyer Zha Ruwei discussed that Wang Han Qing was thinking about money, so they advised Ye to return a little to him, and not to be as short-sighted as them. Ye Fi Kang then said that he had already paid a 20,000 yuan bail to the court, and had a receipt to prove it, and the newspapers had reported it messily. Therefore, he, Zha Ruwei, Cai Ding, Shen Zengkuan published a statement in the newspaper on his behalf to clarify the untrue points, and Wang Han Qing made corrections. However, Wang Han Qing was illiterate. The court believed that he had repeatedly settled with them, but the parties repeatedly demanded it, which was a matter of morality, so he settled. The questioning officer said, "Didn't you tell witnesses Hu Jin Kun and Li Sunshi not to appear in court?" He replied, "No." He was asked whether they had said so during the investigation and trial, and he replied, "This is not my own business, why would I tell them not to come?" At this point, lawyer Gu Ji Rong was asked, "Didn't you say that Wang Han Qing could come to court, why hasn't he come now?" He replied, "Hu Jin Kun has already gone to Hankou to find him." He was asked, "Didn't Wang Han Qing go back to his hometown in Henan?" He replied, "Hu Jin Kun said he can find him." He was asked, "Who introduced Wang Han Qing to you to write the statement?" He replied, "Li Songtang introduced him." He was asked, "Was it to handle a case, or just to write the statement?" He replied, "Just to write the statement." He was asked, "What did he mean to write?" He replied, "He said the money was used by his wife, Zhang, and if the trial continued, it would be unfavorable to him, and he would be guilty of false accusation." He was asked, "Now he is suing, and the defendant is Ye Fu Kang, not him committing a crime, how can he write this statement out of thin air?" He replied, "That is what he meant." He was asked, "Does Wang Han Qing have mental illness?" He replied, "No." He was asked, "Then who came up with the idea to write the statement?" He replied, "He said to make such a statement." The official said, "Wang Han Qing has accused Ye Fu Kang more than once or twice. He himself is willing to admit to false accusations, and he's saying it casually? Is it really his own intention? Before he comes to court, this court cannot believe it." At this point, Ye Fu Kang stated that he was baffled by the words of Li Sunshi, Hu Jin Kun, Wang Han Qing, etc., and that there was no such person as Li Sunshi. The whole thing was fabricated, so Li Sunshi must appear in court. The official ordered that the date be changed and that Wang Han Qing be re-examined when he arrives in court.

### A Quarrel Between Two Children Leads to a Case of Manslaughter; Fellow Villagers Bicker; Xia Cheng Shan Utters a Final Lament

A four-year-old girl named Ai Mao, daughter of Jiangbei woman Zhou Wang (34 years old) residing at No. 401 Saposai Road, French Concession, was squatting on the ground in front of her door urinating at 9:00 AM yesterday, when a ten-year-old boy named Xiang Bao, son of local resident Lu Jin Kui (42 years old, working in a pharmacy) residing at No. 409, passed by and reached out to tease the girl's head. The girl's right arm had a smallpox vaccination that had not yet healed. Touching the vaccination scar caused the girl to cry in pain. Her mother, Zhou Wang, heard the noise from inside the house and came out to investigate. Upon learning that the child had been hurt by the Lu child, she went to the Lu's house to question the Lu child's parents. Both sides began to argue and quarrel, and more than ten neighbors and fellow villagers from both sides gathered, bickering with each other. When they were about to resort to violence, Xia Cheng Shan (approximately 40 years old), a Jiangbei native who pulled a rickshaw and lived at No. 403 on the same road, kindly stepped forward to mediate. Chen Zhi Xiang (36 years old), a Jiangyin native and tailor who lived with the Lu family, worried that Xia was helping the other side, and immediately reached out to stop Xia. Xia lost his balance and fell backward, hitting his head on the door sill, causing a concussion. Yuan Si, a Jiangbei native who lived and worked with Xia, picked Xia up and sent him to Guangci Hospital, but Xia died before receiving medical treatment. The hospital reported to the French Concession police, who sent detectives to the scene to investigate. Lu Jin Kui, Zhou Wang, Chen Zhi Xiang, and others involved were taken to the police station for questioning. After questioning, Lu and Chen were detained pending further investigation. Xia's body was transported to the Tongren Fuyuan branch hall for an autopsy, and a report will be submitted to the Second Special Court tomorrow to send personnel for examination. The deceased was working alone in Shanghai, and his family is in the countryside of Dongtai. His fellow villagers have sent a telegram to notify his family to come to Shanghai to claim the body for burial.

At 10:00 AM on the 25th of this month, a man claiming to be Lu Xin Chang, 29 years old, a local native engaged in the foreign goods business, checked into Room 6 of the Aidoo Hotel at No. 10, Chu Qing Lane, West Xin Qiao Street, French Concession. By noon yesterday, he had not yet gotten up. The tea boy, Xu A Chang (35 years old, from Shaoxing), knocked on the door as usual, asking if the room needed to be extended. To his surprise, there was no response after knocking for a long time. He opened the door and went inside, finding Lu unconscious on the bed, unresponsive, and his face turned pale. Realizing something was wrong, he informed the cashier, who had him taken to Renji Hospital. After the doctor's diagnosis, it was found that Lu had committed suicide by taking poison. ### Zhu Yun Di Denies Divorce, Sues for Bigamy; the Divorce Issue Must be Resolved First; the Trial of Zhuang Ting Gui's Bigamy is Suspended

Zhuang Ting Gui from Wuxi married a woman named Luo Li Li after divorcing his wife, Zhu Yun Di. Zhu suddenly denied that she and Zhuang had separated and sued Zhuang for bigamy in the First Special Court. Therefore, he ordered Zhu to first file a civil suit. ### Ministry of Finance Approves Continued Exemption of Transit Tax on Peanut Oil for Two Years

The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes Trade Association previously requested the Ministry of Finance to continue exempting transit tax on peanuts, peanut kernels, and peanut oil transported domestically from Shanghai for two years, citing the Qingdao precedent to benefit commerce. Yesterday, the association received two approvals from the Ministry of Finance, numbered 11636 and 101, respectively. (1) "Received and noted. The situation in Qingdao and Shanghai is indeed similar to that of Italy and Japan. Therefore, peanuts, peanut kernels, and peanut oil transported from Shanghai to domestic ports should be granted continued exemption from transit tax for two years, following the Qingdao precedent, ending at the end of November 1938. In addition to ordering the Customs Administration to instruct the General Customs Office, this approval is hereby issued for your information." (2) "Received and noted. This case has been submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and a separate approval has been issued. In addition to instructing the General Customs Office to instruct the Jianghai Customs to comply, you are hereby informed."

### Shanghai County Land Bureau Sets Deadline for Collecting Land Title Deeds; Old Documents are Invalid

The Shanghai County Land Administration Bureau has completed the drawing and printing of land ownership certificates and sectional maps for the North Bridge and Great Tree townships in the third district. The distribution will begin on January 2, 1937, for a period of two months. Those who have registered but have not paid the registration fee must pay a registration fee of 2/1000 in addition to the ownership certificate fee. Those who have already paid the registration fee do not need to pay again. The fee for each land ownership certificate is as follows: (1) Land value less than 100 yuan, 20 cents; (2) 100 yuan or more, 50 cents; (3) 500 yuan or more, 1 yuan; (4) 1,000 yuan or more, 2 yuan; (5) 5,000 yuan or more, 5 yuan; (6) 10,000 yuan or more, 10 yuan. If the certificate is collected after the deadline, a storage fee of 10 cents per certificate will be charged for the first month, and 20 cents per certificate for the second month. If the certificate is not collected after the storage fee period expires, the owner will be notified to cancel the registration, and the Land Administration Bureau will temporarily manage it. The Shanghai County Government announced the above measures yesterday, instructing all households to bring their documents to the County Land Administration Bureau within the prescribed period to collect their certificates. It is also reported that the land ownership certificate is a certificate for people's land property, and all subsequent transactions, transfers, or mortgages will be based on the new certificate. All old documents will be invalid.

### Chief of the Yimiao Police Station Disguises Himself to Promote Anti-Drug Campaign, Urging Addicts to Voluntarily Quit Within the Next Few Days

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau intensified and expanded the anti-drug campaign, it has been four days. It was heard yesterday that Yu Pu, the chief of the Yimiao Police Station, will personally lead patrol officer Chen Shu Sheng and dozens of police officers, dressed in disguise, in prosperous areas such as Xiaodongmen, Xinbeimen, Yimiao, Yu Garden, and amusement parks with many tourists, from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM today. They will parade and beat gongs, using two large flags and eight small flags, all writing that those who use drugs such as red pills, white powder, heroin, and gao gen should voluntarily quit within the next few days. If they have not quit by January 1, 1937, they will be shot according to law if caught. They will also warn landlords or sub-landlords not to allow people who manufacture or traffic drugs to live in their houses, and those who know and do not report will be subject to the same punishment. Ten male and female beggars dressed in red, all with execution signs inserted, will participate in the parade and shout slogans to awaken drug addicts.

Xu Xue Seng Sues Zhu Guang Han Case; Gao Jin Sheng Testified Yesterday; Gao Denies His Aunt Wrote the Letter; The Plaintiff's Withdrawal is Suspicious; the Court Orders Xu Xue Seng to be Summoned for Another Interrogation

Xu Xue Seng from Songjiang, who had served as the director of the Gansu Anti-Smoking Bureau and a county magistrate, was severely injured in the French Concession Wang Zhi Road when Gao Jin Sheng splashed nitric acid on him. Gao Jin Sheng was sentenced to four years in prison by the Second Special Court. Zhu claimed that Xu was insatiable in borrowing money and was taking the opportunity to make false accusations. Both sides held their ground, and the trial has been ongoing for a long time without a resolution. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Bo Jun opened the court and brought Gao Jin Sheng from the French Concession for questioning. Gao Jin Sheng testified that he was 25 years old, from Shanghai, lived in Nanyang Bridge, and owned a bicycle shop. He did not know Zhu Guang Han or Chen A Xi, nor was he instigated by them to cause harm. He was asked if he had written a letter to his aunt while in custody, and he replied that he did not have such an aunt at all. The official ordered the handwriting to be compared. Finally, the defendant's defense lawyer stated that the plaintiff had suddenly submitted a statement withdrawing the case, which clearly indicated that there was insufficient evidence and he feared it would be detrimental to him. Gao Jin Sheng, a key witness in the case, also made it clear in his testimony that the facts were clear, and requested that a ruling be made immediately to avoid further litigation. The official ordered Xu Xue Seng to be summoned for another interrogation.

### Zhang Wei Liang's Failure to Pay Alimony Leads to Civil and Criminal Lawsuits; Marriage with Money, but no Money to Repay Debts Puts Dong Mei Zhen in a Difficult Position; a Lawsuit for Damage and a Lawsuit for Objection Keep Zhang Yu Liang Busy

Zhang Wei Liang and Zhang Yu Liang, local natives, had jointly opened a brothers' dental hospital at No. 3, Zhejiang Road, Zhifu Road. Zhang Wei Liang previously married Dong Mei Zhen from Ningbo. They lived together for 13 years and had three children. Last year, Zhang and Dong had a disagreement, which led to litigation. As a result, the court ruled that Zhang and Dong should be divorced and ordered Zhang to pay alimony of 2,160 yuan. After the case was finalized, Zhang failed to pay, resulting in his detention by the court for a month and a half. Zhang then agreed to pay on a monthly basis and was released. However, after regaining his freedom, Zhang went back on his word and married a woman surnamed Xu at the Central Hotel on the 9th of this month, spending thousands of yuan. Dong, seeing Zhang's lavish wedding and his failure to pay the alimony she deserved, requested the First Special Court to seal up Zhang Wei Liang's movable property in the brothers' dental hospital. The court approved the request, and the clerk and bailiff sealed the property on the 14th of this month. When the movable property in Zhang Wei Liang's medical room was to be sealed up, Zhang Wei Liang's copper sign was still hanging at the entrance of the medical room. However, Zhang Yu Liang first expressed an objection to the execution, and then removed the Zhang Wei Liang's copper sign. Therefore, Dong took photos of the traces left on the wall where the copper sign was hung, and accused Zhang Yu Liang of helping to damage her debt claim, filing a complaint with the First Special Court in accordance with Article 356 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday, Judge Dai Rong Duo summoned Zhang Yu Liang to the Second Criminal Court. Zhang Yu Liang testified that although the brothers' dental hospital was nominally jointly organized by his brothers, they actually each handled their own affairs, and the medical rooms were also separated. Later, Wei Liang owed rent, and the landlord sealed up his movable property, which he then bought after the auction. Wei Liang was also hired by him as an assistant. The copper sign was indeed removed by him, because after Wei Liang's marriage on the 9th, there were disagreements, so he was fired. Since he had been fired, the copper sign was removed on the 10th, not when it was sealed on the 14th. He had also filed a lawsuit objecting to the sealing. Dong Mei Zhen claimed that all of this was a deliberate attempt to deceive the court and requested severe punishment according to the law. Judge Dai, after reviewing the testimonies, ordered the end of the debate and set the sentencing for 2:00 PM on the 30th.

### Dr. Ma Song Ting to Return Home Tomorrow; Efforts to Promote Islamic Culture; Expected to Arrive in Shanghai on the 28th

Dr. Ma Song Ting is a well-known Ahong of Islam in our country. In 1925, he and Mr. Tang Ke San, the current member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, founded the Chengda Normal School in Jinan, and later moved it to Beiping. The purpose was to cultivate religious teachers with both new and old knowledge, so as to communicate Chinese and Western cultures. In the past ten years, in addition to being assigned to the Northwest to establish the latest type of primary and secondary schools, the graduates have been sent to Egypt to enter Al-Azhar University, specializing in philosophy and Islamic history and culture. Therefore, the school's achievements have made great strides.

In 1932, Mr. Ma Song Ting traveled to Egypt, and paid homage to the former King Fuad I of Egypt. The King donated thousands of books and specially sent two doctors to China to serve as volunteer professors and agreed to accept as many students as our country sends, with free tuition (food and accommodation are all provided by the Ministry of Education).

In order to commemorate the former King Fuad I of Egypt, the Fuad Library Preparatory Committee was officially established in September this year. The organizers, in addition to the Chengda authorities and famous Muslims, include such cultural giants as Cai Jiemin, Li Shuhua, Weng Wenhao, Xu Bingchang, Gu Zhigang, Feng Youlan, Chen Shuren, Zhang Xinglang, Li Jinxi, Tao Xijian, Bai Pengfei, Yao Congwu, and Chen Yuan, all of whom are members of the preparatory committee and have worked exceptionally hard for the committee.

In order to further strengthen emotional ties, Mr. Ma Song Ting went to Egypt again on October 5th of this year, staying in Cairo for more than a month. He paid homage to the new King Farouk I of Egypt and the Prime Minister of the country, Nahas Pasha, who gave him a warm welcome and promised to send more professors to our country and donate thousands of books to enrich the Fuad Library. He also made very good criticisms of our President Chiang.

During this trip abroad, Mr. Ma carried more than 100 copies of the Three Principles of the People in English and French and distributed them to the Egyptian government and the public. He also lectured on the construction of our country in recent years and the situation of Muslims in our country at the Posai Municipal Government and various cultural organizations in Cairo, which were warmly welcomed by the upper and lower classes of the country's public opinion and cultural circles.

It is reported that Mr. Ma will arrive in Shanghai tomorrow (28th) morning on the Italian ship Conte Verde. It is said that many people are planning to welcome him.

Dr. Ma Song Ting photographed with the Egyptian Prime Minister Nahas at Nahas's private residence (right) Mr. Ma (left) Nahas

### Ningbo Industrial Bank to Resume Business on a Fixed Date; January 9, 1937

The Ningbo Industrial Bank, which has been temporarily closed for more than a year, will resume business officially on January 9, 1937, after the efforts of the people of Ningbo and the telegram from Chairman Chiang to Mr. Yu Qiaqing and other members of the Ningbo Shanghai Association to assist in the vicinity. The bank's board of directors has decided to pay attention to the fishing industry in accordance with Chairman Chiang's instructions after the resumption of business. Zhuang Songfu, a director of the bank and former member of the Legislative Yuan, will be responsible for urging the organization of groups in the fishing area. All preparations have been completed. The Ningbo Shanghai Association has been notified of the progress of the resumption of business, and the matter has been submitted to Chairman Chiang for inspection and approval. In order to save expenses, all branch offices will be merged.

### Anti-Tuberculosis Exhibition Formally Closed Yesterday

The Shanghai First Anti-Tuberculosis Exhibition, jointly organized by the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association and the Jiuzhou Pharmacy, has been open to the public on the second floor of the Wuzhou Building on Fourth Malu since the 15th of this month. The exhibition has been very successful. ### After Running Aground, the Dahua Steamer Safely Arrived in Dinghai Yesterday Morning; to Sail to Shanghai for Repairs on the 30th

After the Dahua steamer of the Ping'an Shipping Company's Shanghai-Taiwan line ran aground at Liuzhu Mountain Mouth, Shuangqikou, Dinghai, the passengers were rescued and safely arrived in Dinghai Ningbo. The cargo was transshipped by the Taizhou steamer to Shanghai. The Shanghai headquarters received a telegram from Manager Li Yaoting from Dinghai at 10:00 AM yesterday, stating, "Dahua floated automatically at 7:00 AM, sailed to Dinghai at 9:00 AM, patched on the beach by welding, set sail on Wednesday, Yao will come tomorrow." The company's original plan to send the Xinbaohua steamer to tow the ship has been abandoned. After the Dahua steamer arrives in Shanghai, it will be repaired at the Laogongmao Shipyard.

### Zhao Shu Sheng Passed Away Yesterday

Zhao Shu Sheng, a standing committee member of the National Postal Workers' Union, a standing director of the China Labor Association, and a school board member and secretary-general of the Minli Middle School, was talented, knowledgeable, and had served in the postal and education sectors for many years. He devoted himself to the postal workers' movement and made outstanding contributions. In recent years, he has also been engaged in educational work, which has been particularly arduous. He unfortunately passed away at his residence in Shanghai at 9:45 AM yesterday due to overwork. Relatives and friends were saddened by the news and rushed to offer condolences. The family has moved Mr. Zhao's remains to the Shanghai Funeral Home on Xiexu Road. Relatives and friends Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, and others have organized a funeral committee to handle the funeral. The encoffining is scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 28th of this month.

Kidnapping a Married Woman: Man and Woman Each Sentenced to Months in Prison - Mrs. Yang Wang and Her Husband Estranged - Chen Gongjian Takes Advantage to Entice

A young woman from Haizhou, Yang Wang (also known as Xiuying), residing in a bungalow on Huasheng Road, worked in a cotton mill. Recently, she had frequent quarrels with her husband, Yang Qingyuan, and often confided in her neighbor and fellow townsman, Wang Jinbiao. Wang harbored malicious intentions, and on October 22nd at 5 PM, he seized the opportunity to incite her to run away. She took all her clothes and jewelry and went with him to a hotel upstairs in the French Concession’s Yong'an Street, where Chen Gongjian from Qingjiang, a friend of Wang's, resided. Wang Jinbiao claimed that she was his goddaughter, and they hid her there for a month. They conspired with Chen to take her to another port to sell her, but because they couldn't find a buyer and feared detection by the French police, they moved to a certain address on Fuyou Road in the Chinese district to stay temporarily. They told the woman that there was a factory in Nanjing with good wages. In reality, they had plotted to trick her into going to Nanjing and then selling her to Fujian to split the profits. However, detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau found out about their plan. On the 16th, Chen Gongjian was arrested. Yang Wang took the opportunity to escape. Chen confessed that she lived in a bungalow on Huasheng Road in the International Settlement. The bureau dispatched detectives to the Yulin Road police station to assist Chief Detective Chen Yonggui in secretly arresting Wang Jinbiao at the address. He was sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday morning, the police brought Chen back and sent him and Wang Jinbiao to the Third Criminal Court. Labor Bureau lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated that Yang Wang had returned home, testified, and requested severe punishment according to the law. According to Mrs. Yang’s statement, she was deceived by Wang Jinbiao, who wanted to trick her into being sold in Fujian. Her husband, Yang Qingyuan, also testified about his wife’s disappearance. Questioned about this, the two defendants gave evasive answers. Judge Zhong Qing sentenced Wang Jinbiao and Chen Gongjian to six months of imprisonment each as a warning.

Shanghai's Electrical Manufacturing Industry (Continued)

— Chief Editor of China WeChat

(Overview of Shanghai Industry and Commerce, Part 40)

According to our agency’s comprehensive survey, the business situation of electrical materials in Shanghai last year was generally sluggish in the spring. With the gradual lengthening of foreign exchange rates, manufacturers with large inventories even reported significant losses. The closure of Shanghai Bulb Company in March was a result of this influence. However, the downward trend reversed after autumn, further impacted by the Italo-Ethiopian War and the new currency system. Material prices rose sharply, allowing those with large inventories to more than make up for the losses of the first half of the year. Companies such as Huitong, Hongkang, Xiefeng, and Tianfaxie all achieved profits. Regarding the production and sales of the light bulb industry in Shanghai over the past year, according to a survey conducted by the Greater American Evening Post among manufacturers in the industry, the highest output was from the Ya'er Bulb Factory, reaching 2 million units, with a business value of 400,000 yuan. Followed by Huade Factory, although its output was less than Ya'er Bulb Factory, the number of high-voltage bulbs it produced was greater, so its business volume exceeded the former by more than 600,000 yuan. However, both were lower than the previous year. At the same time, due to oversupply, some bulb prices fell below cost. In the twenty-third year, the selling price of ordinary bulbs was 32-33 yuan per hundred, but last year it once fell to about 10 yuan. Shenbao reported slightly different figures, stating that the total output of bulbs from various bulb factories in Shanghai last year was over 16 million units, with Ya'er accounting for one-third, or over 5 million units, which is more than 3 million units higher than the previous statement. The highest selling price for ordinary bulbs was 22 yuan per hundred, and the lowest was 8 yuan. Both are for reference.

Charity Football Tournament: Donghua Loses to French Businessmen 0-2 - Mayor Wu Personally Kicks Off, Presents Awards, and Auctions Old Ball

The annual Charity Cup football tournament, traditionally held on Christmas, was brought forward one day this year and took place yesterday afternoon at 3 PM in Shenyuan. The audience was not particularly large. Due to recent unrest, people are apprehensive. Although the ticket revenue from the football field has not been precisely tallied, it is estimated to be around 2,000 yuan. During the match, Donghua was at a disadvantage in the first half due to playing against the wind, leading to the loss of one goal, scored by French player Fafanxiao. The first half was 22-11, and the Women's Middle School team's forwards were closely guarded in the second half, and they only scored two goals in the whole half, resulting in a 45-13 victory for Dongya. Dongya won five out of five matches in Hangzhou and returned to Shanghai in triumph last night by train.

Three industrial and commercial football matches were held at the Municipal Sports Ground yesterday afternoon: (1) In the Group One final, Weixin and Jin Xing both forfeited; (2) In Group One of the gods, the Public Security Bureau did not attend and forfeited to Ying Guang; (3) In Group Two of the gods, Chang Geng played against Fei Gong. Educational News

Citywide Youth and Students Held Grand Celebration Meeting for Chairman Yesterday

Two thousand middle school and university students and vocational youths attended. Director Pan gave a speech on Chairman's great personality and influence. Various cultural groups sent congratulatory telegrams to celebrate.

Over two thousand youth and students from major middle schools and universities in the city held a celebration meeting at Lake Society at 5 pm yesterday. Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, was specially invited to attend and give a speech. The situation was enthusiastic. Details are as follows:

Participating schools included Jinda, Fudan, Daxia, Guanghua, Tongji, Jiaotong, Datong, Hujiang, Business School, Medical School, Sino-French, Political Science, Law School, Soochow, Chizhi, Zhengfeng, Tongde, Southeast, Shanghai Art School, Zhonggong, New China, East Asia, Hujiang Business School, Mongolian-Tibetan School, Qingxin, Wuben, Nursery Teacher, Zhi Ren Yong, Peicheng, China, Peiming, Zhixing, Jinan, Affiliated Middle School, East China, Daxia Affiliated Middle School, Fudan Middle School, Hujiang Affiliated Middle School, Jingye, Xinlu Minli, Private Shanghai, Pudong, Qingnian, Nanyang, Lida, Zhengfeng and other schools. Students Li Qingxin, Wang Kemai, Zhong Huanxin, Liu Shuming, Yao Jitang, Zhou Ren, Li Lianzhu, Sha Rongcun, Ma Xiongcai, Shi Maojun, Wang Zhongyao, Song Enrong, Qiu Youxin, Ji Hanzhang, and others, more than two thousand people in total, publicly elected Jinan, Guanghua, Jiaotong, Fudan and other schools as the presidium.

Celebration Order: (1) Stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National flags, and the portrait of the Premier and the Leader; (4) Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) Silence; (6) Chairman reports; (7) Director Pan delivers a speech; (8) Speeches; (9) Shout slogans; (10) Fire cannons; (11) Have a meal together.

Director's Speech: Director Pan Gongzhan said in his speech, "Comrades, today is the happiest day for our entire country. Our leader's fiftieth birthday. When Shanghai's school youth and students celebrated the leader, they once said that our revolutionary leader's work has made great contributions in the recent period. On the 12th of this month, when Zhang Xueliang hijacked him in Xi'an, we heard the news and unanimously condemned the rebels. We believed that he could get out of danger safely and continue to exercise his functions. Now that we have our leader back safely, the grief we felt in those ten days has turned into joy, fully expressing our support for the leader. From this Xi'an Incident and the return of our leader, we can see three forces: (1) the power of the leader's great and noble personality to influence people. Our national revival has been fully revealed from this incident. Today's celebration is not only to celebrate the leader's return, but also to celebrate the national revival. We must recognize that our leader went to Xi'an knowing it was dangerous, but he did not avoid the danger. This shows our leader's courage. The whole country already knows about Zhang Xueliang's conspiracy and advised the leader not to go. Our leader was not afraid of death and wanted to use his great personality to move people who could not be moved, so he went to Xi'an. Unexpectedly, Zhang Xueliang, with the heart of a wolf, could not only not be moved, but also hijacked him. The first thing our leader did in the siege was to make Zhang Xueliang moved by the leader's diary. At the same time, when Zhang Xueliang repeatedly decided to see him, the leader said to him, 'You call me Chairman, which means you are my subordinate, and you should send me back to Beijing. If you want to threaten me, you are a rebel and you can kill me immediately.' This is also the greatness of the leader. Finally, the leader wrote a letter to Minister He to stop the bombing, not sacrificing the people for personal reasons. Furthermore, as soon as he arrived in Luoyang, he ordered a halt to military action. This kind of great and noble personality, although it cannot completely move Zhang Xueliang, can at least make him realize the greatness of the leader's personality. (2) The power of national unity. Although the hijacking was unfortunate, it provided a test, which proved that except for a very small number of traitors and communists, all 450 million people in the country unanimously supported the leader and condemned the rebels. This unprecedented great test proves the strength of China. This kind of force is enough to overthrow any huge turmoil, let alone a Zhang Xueliang. This incident has attracted the attention of countries all over the world, who are watching how China responds to this incident to determine whether the Chinese nation can revive. Let's look at the enthusiastic and joyful scene last night, and the expressions of pain and anger in the previous few days. It is simply that everyone, regardless of age, gender, or class, is united. This united and great force is enough to prove that China has reached the time of roaring, and the national revival will definitely succeed. (3) The power of a sound government organization. People say that we are unorganized, but this test proves that our government is organized and does not waver because one person has lost his freedom. Therefore, after the leader was hijacked, the central government's first step was to dismiss and severely punish, and the second step was to order a crusade. The steps were clear and the system was not chaotic, which shows that our government has an absolutely sound organization. Zhang Xueliang hijacked the leader entirely as a means of coercion, thinking that we would definitely be constrained. However, the government's decision was to not be constrained. The power of such a government with a sound organization can overcome the rebels. In short, the test of this incident proves that China has a leader with a great personality, a united people, and a government with a sound organization. The combination of these three forces is a modern country. We have all the conditions, so China is already a modern country. Therefore, today we celebrate the leader's escape from danger, and at the same time, we celebrate that our nation has embarked on the road to revival."

After cheers and discussion, it was decided that the representative of Jinan Affiliated Middle School would give a speech, and the whole audience shouted slogans. In the evening, everyone had a meal together, and there was also a variety show performance.

Grain: Imported Wheat Prices Continue to Rise Unabated; Flour and Wheat Rise Together

Flour Rises Seven or Eight Cents; Wheat Jumps One Jiao Six

Flour Yesterday Flour, after the morning, prices in each month showed a uniform rising trend. As the price of imported wheat, Chicago, continued to rise by one yuan, because the rising wind of imported wheat was terrible, and because Chairman Jiang Weiyuan had escaped from danger, most people naturally felt more enthusiastic. The rate of increase in each month ranged from four or five cents to eight cents. As buying was slightly quiet, there was a slight loosening. Until the afternoon opening, the people's hearts in January have been settled, and the long-term trend because buying is still strong, increased by one or two points. The current market situation, because domestic wheat has no ability to control, such as imported wheat rising and not planning, investors seem to have no intention to stop.

Wheat Yesterday's futures wheat market, the morning opening, each month rose sharply, because imported wheat continued to rise by one yuan to one yuan and five or six jiao, this rebound, is also out of expectation. When the price was opened, because this month is the last day of trading, the initial opening was only six yuan and six jiao half, and the degree was still quiet, but when filming the long-term, although the transaction was clear, the price has shouted eight or nine points, and then stopped. Until the afternoon opening, the flour market skyrocketed, and this month is the last few sets, the holders are prepared to recover, the price then continued to rise, and the long-term is more difficult because the exit is more restrained, and the buying is more upright, so it also increased by six or seven points. Calculated the increase during the day, from one jiao to one jiao six points, the current wheat market, because the standard has risen for two consecutive days, customers naturally sell, but the factory stomach is still not very greedy, only opened Jiangbei wheat six yuan and seven jiao half, a total of more than four thousand packages, was handled by Fu and Fu two companies.

Children's Special Edition of Shen Bao

Cotton Yarn

Yarn Prices Once Soared, Affected by the Tri-Product Market Surge, Ultimately Falling Due to Swaps and Liquidations

Initially, the yarn market in Osaka saw a surge of 12 yuan in cotton yarn prices. It was said that the frequent rise in cotton yarn prices was due to the import of 800,000 bales of Australian wool in the coming year, along with Japan exporting 153.7 million square yards of goods. Consequently, yarn prices soared, causing anxiety in the local market and driving strong buying interest and price increases. However, as the year-end approached and the February futures delivery was ample, many sellers emerged, loosening the market and shifting the trend downward. Nevertheless, some bulls remained optimistic about the forward market.

A Loss of Over Two Yuan in January Yarn Alone

The opening price of the January yarn futures market was calm, as the December delivery had a substantial 7,700 bales, suppressing market sentiment. However, news from the Osaka tri-product yarn market caused a surge of 12 yuan in all months. This suddenly boosted buying interest, with the February contract jumping by [blank] yuan and 70 cents, and the March contract rising by 3 yuan and 88 cents. In the second round of trading, Changfeng and Yuda heavily sold near-term contracts, softening the market and dropping prices by 10 cents to [blank] yuan and 90 cents. However, spot yarn business remained robust. By the third closing, the market was flat, with January rising only 30 cents compared to the previous day's close, and the far-month rising 1 yuan and 20 cents to [blank] yuan and 50 cents. In the afternoon session, rumors spread that a certain merchant and company were swapping out of the market, further weakening market sentiment. The forward market was also affected, with prices steadily declining. As a result, all months fell by 2 yuan, 50 cents, 60 cents to 1 yuan and 30 cents compared to the morning closing. It was found that Yuda sold 5,350 bales, Gengfeng 1,900 bales, Xingchang 1,100 bales, Changfeng 3,300 bales, Mingde 1,650 bales, and RunKang 1,050 bales. Buyers included [blank] Ji 1,100 bales, [blank] Fu 800 bales, Tong Ji 1,350 bales, Hengsheng [blank] thousand and 300 bales, Shen Ji 1,050 bales, Wang Taixing and [blank] each 400 bales, Dachangcheng 1,300 bales, Xiesheng 900 bales, Fukang 850 bales, and Taichang 1,200 bales. The highest and lowest prices of the day are listed on the left.

Thread Prices Rise by Five Yuan

Spot yarn sales are still good. It is found that all guilds bought a total of 875 bales throughout the day, with sales prices rising by 2 yuan and thread prices rising by 5 yuan. The purchase volume of each guild is listed below:

Guangdong: [blank] 220, [blank] 510; Xiamen: [blank] 5

Shantou: [blank] 55; Hankou: [blank] 15; Luzhou: [blank] 40

Sichuan: [blank] 30

Cotton Prices Lack Momentum, Falling with the Yarn Market

Initially, cotton prices rose due to the consistent increases in overseas [blank] American [blank] and the Osaka tri-product market surge of 2 to [blank] 3 yuan [blank], raising market sentiment and driving prices higher. However, in the afternoon, the cotton market was drawn into the vortex of the declining yarn market and steadily declined.

Spot Cotton Prices Fall by Around Ten Cents

The opening price of the spot cotton market was bullish due to the surge in the Osaka tri-product cotton market by 2 yuan, 78 cents to 3 yuan, and the consistent increase in American and Indian cotton prices. All months rose uniformly, jumping by 60-70 cents. However, as the yarn market retreated, the cotton market was constrained. As a result, all months rose by 25 to 30 cents compared to the previous day's closing. In the afternoon session, market sentiment was weak, and prices steadily declined due to the weakness of the yarn market and floating profits being liquidated. [blank] however, daily [blank] all fell by 35 to 40 cents. It was found that [blank] Tong sold 5,200 [blank], [blank] Feng 3,500 dan, Dafeng 1,700 dan, Jinchang 2,600 dan, Daqing 2,000 dan, Changji 3,400 dan, Wang Taixing 1,700 dan, Dachang 6,500 dan, Shengyuan 4,000 dan, Changhe 10,300 dan, Xingchang 1,200 dan, RunKang 4,000 dan, Hengyi 4,200 dan, Taixing 2,200 dan, Changfeng Bafeng 600 dan, Yikang 5,700 dan, Daji 2,800 dan, Hexing 1,800 dan, Taichang 3,100 dan, and Yichang 2,300 dan. The highest and lowest prices of the day are listed on the left.

Factories Continue to Purchase Spot Cotton

Spot cotton consumption is still good, with factories continuing to make sporadic transactions. The source is 1,100 bales of Yao cotton and 890 bales of Tong cotton.

Cotton Futures Also Rose by Over Three Yuan

Osaka telegram on the 26th: Tri-product futures yarn rose by 9 yuan, 60 cents to 13 yuan. The near-month contract was 262 yuan, 70 cents, and the far-month was 25 [blank] yuan, [blank] 80 cents.

"To Do Great Things, First Set Great Ambitions"

The Story of Lincoln Growing a Beard

— Te

Isn't the portrait of President Lincoln, the American emancipator of slaves, that we see every day, full of beard? In fact, he didn't grow a beard until he became president at the age of 51. The reason he grew a beard has a small story. When the United States was electing a president in 1860, Lincoln was the Republican presidential candidate. For publicity purposes, the Republican Party posted his portraits all over the streets. An eleven-year-old girl accidentally saw Lincoln's face in the portrait, which was shaved clean, and thought to herself that a country's president shouldn't be solemn without a beard. So she wrote a letter to Lincoln, which read: "Dear Mr. Lincoln, I think you would look much better with a beard. I have four brothers, two Republicans and two Democrats. If you listen to me and grow a beard, I think I can persuade my two Democratic brothers to vote for you." Lincoln received the letter and wrote back: "Thank you for your kindness, but if I listen to you and grow a beard right away, don't you think I'll be laughed at for being infatuated?" Later, Lincoln was elected president. One day, when he was taking a train to West Town in Washington State, where the little girl lived, he sent someone to bring the little girl to him. As soon as he saw her coming, he jumped off the train, walked through the crowd, and sat with her next to the station platform. He pointed to his face and said, "Little [one], look, didn't I grow [it]? I grew it for you." With that, he gave her a warm kiss. But from then until Lincoln was assassinated, they never met again. The little girl regarded this as supreme glory, kept it firmly in her heart, and often talked about it to others. Who was the little girl? She was Mrs. Pillings, an 88-year-old woman from Telleffos Town, Kansas, who recently passed away.

Plants

— Zhen

One day, Min'er unintentionally pulled up a small tree. He didn't even know why he pulled it up. But he stared at the tree blankly and said to himself, a tree always has these three parts: root, stem, and leaves. What are these three parts for? This strange opening question made him unable to answer. This kind of question that he couldn't answer was often discovered unintentionally.

"Brother, look, eight or nine out of ten trees in the world have these three parts: root, stem, and leaves. What are these three parts for?"

"Yes, almost all plants have these three parts. Not only are there the root, stem, and leaf parts, but the more advanced plants also have the flower, fruit, and seed parts. The root, stem, leaf, flower, fruit, and seed are all called organs. The root, stem, and leaf are called vegetative organs, and the flower, fruit, and seed are called reproductive organs. These six organs all have special structures and functions, but their structures cannot be seen by our naked eyes, and each organ cooperates to maintain the life of the plant. Speaking of the functions of the six organs, you can know if you think carefully. I might as well tell you first: the root, usually the roots grow in the soil, but there are also those that grow in water and air, but these are just exceptions. The function of the roots growing in the soil is twofold: (1) To absorb water and minerals dissolved in the water from the soil and transport them to the stem, (2) To enable the part of the plant on the ground to stand upright firmly in the air, (3) Store the nutrients already made in the leaves. Stem: The stem grows in the air. Its functions are four. (1) Spread the leaves in the air so that each leaf receives enough sunlight, because the leaves can make more nutrients in the sunlight. (2) Continue to transport the water and dissolved minerals sent by the roots to the leaves. (3) Transport the nutrients that have been manufactured in the leaves to all parts of the plant body, (4) Store nutrients for a long or short period of time. Leaves: Leaves all grow on the stem. The main function is to make food. Flowers, fruits, and seeds are all for plants to produce small plants and extend their race. However, these six organs are only found in higher plants.

What are higher plants?

"Plants can be divided into major categories: (1) Seed plants. These are all propagated by planting seeds. They are the most advanced class in the plant kingdom and have a close relationship with humans. (2) Ferns: They have roots, stems, and leaves, but their method of reproduction is still fern spores. A spore is just a particle. Producing this spore does not require flowering procedures, so it is lower than seed plants. (3) Mosses: Most grow in water or shady and damp places, but have no roots. (4) Algae and fungi plants: These are the lowest-level plants, the structure is very simple, and there is no distinction between roots, stems, and leaves."

Strange Water Spider

— Zhong Mei

"Brother Min, what is that thing in the water over there?" Little Yong asked in surprise, flashing his eyes, while pointing his little finger at the thing in the water. Brother Min looked for a while, then answered him: "Brother Yong, that's probably a water spider."

"Then what do they use to breathe in the water? Are they like fish using gills and humans using lungs?"

"Their breathing apparatus is extremely strange, and it is not like fish breathing with gills or we humans breathing with lungs, but with a kind of air storage room. This air storage room is oblong, and the opening is at the bottom. They don't have to work hard to build it, they just need to use the viscous silk in their abdomen to make it. They transport air using the bubble method. After they climb to the surface of the water, they use a pair of feet to stroke, and they make a small bubble. Then they put the bubble in the middle of their feet and clamp it into the water. After storing the gas, they break the bubble, and the gas rises into the air storage room. After doing this more than ten times, the air storage room is filled with fresh air."

"What kind of work do they do in the summer?"

"The work they have to do in the summer is to reproduce. The number of water spider eggs is often very large, some have thousands and hundreds. They put them inside a shell made of silk. After not much time, these eggs turn into small water spiders, and crawl out of the silk shell. After not much time, they can also build air storage rooms and transport fresh air.

"Brother Min, what are they used for?"

"Their usefulness is also great. They often help us catch mosquitoes and poisonous flies on the water surface, so they are also very beneficial animals."

Snail Encirclement of Centipede

— Pillow

According to common sense [blank] judgment: The centipede is one of the famous five poisonous creatures, that is, it has [blank] long body and the most healthy feet. The so-called "a hundred-legged worm dies but does not fall," how could there be a standard weak insect, the snail, that is less than an inch long, moves slowly, and is regarded as being incapable of anything [blank] conquering it? I was always surprised that when we Jiangnan people occasionally saw a centipede crawling nearby, we wanted to kill it immediately to avoid future troubles, but we were afraid of poisoning the skin by catching it with our hands, so we often used a superstitious curse method, chanting: "Land slug land slug land slug..." Saying this repeatedly, [blank] it is said to be very effective, and it will naturally make the centipede's white limbs weak and its crawling sluggish. It gives people time to find a weapon of attack and kill it. It turns out that the land slug is the common name of the snail; I don't know why the centipede is so afraid of the snail, even to the point of being terrified at the mention of its name? After my brother-in-law, the physician Zhou Mingxin, witnessed a heart-pounding invasion battle, it can accurately explain that their restraint comes from a reason.

One night, Zhou Jun inadvertently caught sight of a large centipede on the base of the wall, arching its body almost bent and sticking together, supporting it with only the feet on both sides of the head and tail. This spectacle led Zhou Jun to carry a lamp and look closer. He then saw a snail near the centipede, leisurely continuing its work of circling. The viscous liquid left behind where it traveled sparkled with a spiral line. The circle surrounding it further away was looser, clearly [blank] visible. Under the circumstances of the snail slowly crawling on the wall in a situation that was slow but unceasing, circling smaller and smaller, closer and closer, this was truly not far-fetched, the centipede's tiptoed feet were standing closer and closer, and the towering body was bent tighter and tighter. The shaky tower-like body became top-heavy, and it finally failed to maintain its position and collapsed. At the same time, its life disappeared without any physiological recovery!

It turns out that the centipede is most afraid of the viscous liquid excreted by the snail. Not only does it not dare to touch it slightly, but it also feels uncomfortable smelling the odor. What is strange is that the snail will know how the centipede is, and then it will start its tactics. From afar, it seems to be carelessly walking around the big circle with its viscous liquid, gradually circling closer. The centipede relies on its venom to run rampant and recklessly, and suddenly it will retreat without stopping when it approaches the liquid line left by the snail. After this experience, it is determined to avoid it from afar. At first, it was still carefree, but it never knew that its body had fallen into a heavy siege and could not move a step. In the end, it was trapped inside, with no place to live, to the point of death.

In this way, the little snail should not be underestimated.

Di'er Is Sick

— Chonglou

Di'er is my niece. She has a pair of bright eyes and a lively personality. I once wrote an article introducing her to the little readers of this publication.

I was separated from Di'er for several years. When I returned to my hometown this year, Di'er's body had grown a lot, and she was no longer a child who wanted me to hold her. However, her temperament was still so lively. Whenever she saw me, she always wanted me to hang her on my arm and rotate her like an airplane.

Later, we went to travel to Mount Hua, and we also took Di'er with us. Di'er was not afraid of the dangerous road. She ran and jumped on the mountain road [blank], refusing to ride in a sedan chair, and climbed the iron rope with us all the way to the precipitous ridge of Qianchi Zhang.

But since I returned to Shanghai, I have received several letters from my hometown in succession, all saying that Di'er was sick, and that she had a fever and cough every day... I'm afraid it's [blank] early stage tuberculosis! This news made me very anxious. I wanted to see her illness but couldn't. I could only write letters to my family to teach them to take good care of her and treat her. Now I always have to remember her bright eyes in my heart!

Little readers! Do you also miss Di'er's illness? Then I hope you pay attention to hygiene and don't let your body get sick.

Preparation

— Householder

The weather is gradually getting colder, and the ants are busily searching for food to prepare for their winter. One day, Brother Ant found a dead fly on the ground and slowly dragged it back to the nest.

On the way, he met his former neighbor, the golden beetle.

"Hello, Brother Ant? Why are you so busy all day long?" the golden beetle asked smugly.

"Hey! Hello, Brother! The weather has been getting colder these past few days, so I'm looking for some things to eat in the winter," the ant said.

"Ugh! You're so silly! Look at me, running around all day with nothing to do, how comfortable! You're always working, you're such a fool, such a fool, haha..." The golden beetle laughed proudly for a while and walked away.

Brother Ant watched its back, shook his head and sighed, and continued to drag the food back to the nest.

The northwest wind grew stronger day by day, the leaves were all blown away, and no one knew what the outside situation was like. Brother Ant took advantage of the good sunshine to go out for a walk and met the golden beetle lying on the ground, unable to move.

The Fox and the White Goose

— Zhang Yizhi

One day, a fox was extremely hungry and walked to the riverbank. He saw a white goose in the river and wanted to eat it.

He tricked the white goose, saying: "Friend, I have good news for you: the birds and beasts had a meeting on the mountain the day before yesterday and decided that they should not kill each other from now on. Therefore, there is a celebration today on the mountain. I have come specially to invite you to participate. Come with me quickly!"

The white goose heard this and thought: "The fox is a famous trickster, this may not be a good intention." So it stretched its neck, looked ahead, and ignored the fox.

After a while, the fox said impatiently: "What are you looking at? Why do you keep looking and ignoring me? Are you going or not?"

The white goose suddenly showed a panicked look and said: "I see two dogs wagging their tails and walking quickly towards here!"

The fox was most afraid of dogs. When he heard that dogs were coming, he was extremely frightened. His body couldn't help but tremble, and he wanted to run away.

The white goose laughed: "Mr. Fox, didn't you just say that the birds and beasts have already decided not to kill each other from now on? Why are you still afraid of dogs?"

We can learn three lessons from the above fable:

One: To live in society, one must be honest. Deceptive methods cannot gain people's trust and will only lose one's own credibility.

Two: When hearing something, one must examine whether it is reliable and not believe it lightly.

Three: The white goose's distrust of the fox's words is the white goose's prudence; the white goose's use of a trick to test the fox's truthfulness is the white goose's alertness.

A Letter to All the Children of the Nation

— Wu Pinxian, Fifth Grader of Zhiben Elementary School

Dear children of the nation: Recently, the puppet bandit army has been invading Suiyuan, using many airplanes and cannons to attack day and night. The soldiers defending the land of Suiyuan, in the freezing weather, carrying long guns on their backs, holding big knives in their hands, not afraid of hunger and cold, not hesitating to sacrifice, are fighting with the enemy for the country and striving for glory for the nation. How should we admire and respect their spirit!

You must know that Suiyuan is not the Suiyuan of the Suiyuan soldiers, nor is it the Suiyuan of the Suiyuan people. It is the Suiyuan of the people of the whole country. Everyone should protect it. We children, although we are still young, cannot fight on the battlefield, but our patriotism should not lag behind others. We should also bear the responsibility of providing support in the rear. I hope that all the children of the nation will unite to aid Suiyuan, save the money for buying candies and toys every day, collect it together, and transfer it to the heroic soldiers at the front as their needs. I hope that children, from now on, quickly save money and take on our responsibilities! I won't write much more, goodbye! I wish you progress!

Sister Wu Pinxian respectfully on December 3,

The Benefits of Reading Newspapers

— Cheng Ming

Children: In addition to your daily schoolwork, you need to read more newspapers, because the news and articles published on the newspapers can increase your general knowledge and help the progress of your studies. For example, international news can help you understand the general trends of the world, domestic news can help you know the major events of the country and the various things in provinces, counties, and districts. Local news is related to the construction, finance, education, sports, and other important events in the city area. Moreover, the supplements of various newspapers have children's works, and you can exchange knowledge in children's works, which is a very beneficial and interesting thing! And the prices of various newspapers are also very cheap. In addition to cutting out the articles in the newspaper supplements and pasting them into booklets for reference, you can also sell the old newspapers to get a value equal to three-tenths of the newspaper price. If you want to save money and be economical, then there is a very good method that everyone can try. You only need to contact a few children and organize a small newspaper reading club. Each month, each person only needs to take out a few dimes to subscribe to several beneficial newspapers, and everyone can take turns reading them. That is a good and economical way to benefit a lot!

Filial Piety (10)

— Hai

This was a joyful Easter Sunday. In that Greek chapel, all those with differing opinions had come to reconcile. When people met each other, Jide greeted them with a smile, saying, "Jesus Christ is risen." On the other hand, they also replied: "He is truly risen." Then they kissed each other, and even if there were any differences of opinion, they were completely forgotten at this time.

Berth Schofield was talking to Yi when he told him about his coming to plead for his father; that gentleman paid close attention to Yi and quickly introduced Yi to him, Yi told him about his coming to plead for his father. The gentleman paid close attention to Yi, showed great sympathy for Yi, but earnestly said to Yi: "It is useless to appeal to the Upper House; because even if Yi can get help from the Upper House to re-examine Yi's father's case, it will be very troublesome and time-consuming, and there is no guarantee that it will be overturned; so it is better to directly appeal to Emperor Alexander, if he is willing to show a compassionate heart, then the goal will be achieved."

Berth Schofield happily returned to the merchant, smiling and saying that this time it was really necessary to thank the Peter the Great statue, because if he hadn't looked at him at that time, Yi would not have noticed that the Neva River had thawed. At this moment, the merchant happened to return from Riga and knew that there was no progress in Berth Sfield's matter, so he immediately took Yi to see that Lord Ti, the lord was an old lady who received Berth Schofield very kindly and left Yi to live in Laili. But for several days in a row, the lord's residence was always holding lively banquets, everyone was playing cards, the old lord and the general guests had forgotten Berth Schofield's mission, poor Yi was always in the house every day, wandering around, very anxious in his heart, feeling that the infinite hope was afraid of disappointment. Yi remembered that the lord had advised Yi to see a Mr. Wei, who was the secretary of the Empress Dowager Mary and would definitely find a way for Yi. So the prisoner was taken to Mr. Wei's house, Mr. Wei happened to be not at home, but he already knew that Yi was coming to him, thinking that he was from a poor family and seeking Zhouji, so he left fifty rubles in advance for Yi to take back. Mrs. Wei saw Yi, and was very happy, listened to Yi's account of the past and present, was very moved, and kept Yi to wait for Mr. Wei to come back. After Mr. Wei came back, he knew about this and also expressed enthusiastic sympathy, and immediately rushed to see the Empress Dowager. Her old man was also one of the most gentle and charitable women in the world. Ordered Mr. Wei to bring Berth Schofield to see her every night. The poor girl turned pale when she heard the good news, and her eyes were full of tears. She didn't have time to thank Mr. Wei, and shouted to the sky: "My God, I have always trusted you, and it is not wrong in the end." At that moment, Yi kissed Mrs. Wei's hand and shouted; "Madam, you must accept my thanks, because your slave husband has saved my father!"

Berth Schofield didn't care what clothes she was wearing, nor did she care about the etiquette of meeting the Empress Dowager: Yi's simple heart only had the wish to plead for her father. Mrs. Wei only tidied up Yi's clothes and asked the prisoner to follow Mr. Wei. As soon as Berth Schofield saw the palace in front of her, she said happily: "If my father sees me now, how happy he will be! My God, complete your work!"
