Supplement to the Shenbao Local Edition Amateur Weekly

Interviews with Celebrities

Returning to Beijing Zhou from the Suiyuan Front Lines

— Jingcha

Mr. Chong Jingzhou decided to go to the front lines to preside over the rescue of wounded soldiers in Suiyuan, without regard for the long journey and the hardships of swimming in the snowy weather. When he returned from the front lines, familiar people from the community went to visit him and inquired diligently about the situation of the wounded soldiers. Introduced by Ms. Hu Huiru, I also went to visit Mr. Pang. Mr. Pang was tall and burly, with thick eyebrows and big eyes, and spoke fluent old Beijing dialect. His kind and approachable attitude reminded me that I had also seen him during the "January 28th" Shanghai War, but I had not spoken to him directly. At that time, he and Dr. Ding Huikang worked very hard to serve the wounded soldiers fighting against the enemy in Shanghai.

"You must have worked really hard this time!"

"No, doctors are supposed to rescue people, especially the soldiers who are fighting for our nation!"

"How is the situation on the front lines?"

"You must have seen the talks I published in the newspapers. Looking at the current situation, I feel that rescue work is very important!"

"I heard that you want to organize a large-scale rescue team to go to the front lines again. When can it be realized?"

"This is the training class organized by the Training Promotion Association of the Rescue Cause Association. It can be said that it is entirely organized for the rescue of the wounded in Suiyuan. At the same time, there are many rescue classes organized by the outside world in the association that are stepping up training. Once they have completed the necessary knowledge, they will go to serve. But now the association has decided to do it themselves. Now we will set up a school first, temporarily located at Chengdu Road and Anxiao Elementary School. And the association has entrusted me with the responsibility of hiring teachers, and it will start in a few days. Now the admitted students have been notified separately."

"Are there any donations for the application of medicines and bandages, etc.?"

"This time is no less than the "January 28th"! As long as someone advocates or explains that it is a necessity, people will donate a large amount. When I just came back from the front lines this time, I just casually talked a little about the needs of the front lines, such as cold protection, anti-poison, etc., and in a few days, a lot of them had been collected and transported to the front lines. This has been reported in the newspaper, and I don't need to report the numbers again!"

"How much medicine and other things have been donated in total?"

"The association is organized with a drug supply committee. According to statistics, pharmacies in the city have generously donated about 130,000 first aid kits, which was just three or four days ago. In addition, many were sent directly to the Red Cross from various places. It's really impossible to count!"

"I think the rescue work at the front lines is probably very difficult, right?"

"Of course it is very difficult, but sometimes the inspiration of the spirit can overcome everything. Even in freezing weather, often below zero degrees, those engaged in work are still full of enthusiasm and do not shrink back and cannot do things. However, in order to strengthen the work, we pay attention to mental training and common sense issues in training rescue talents."

When he said this, he gave me a very strong impression. On his face, which still had the color of dust, the ruddy color shone through his yellow skin, and his thick black beard and eyebrows showed solemnity and majesty, but also extreme peace and calmness. I further asked him;

"What is mental training?"

"The work of rescuing the wounded on the front lines is completely different from the situation of peacetime nursing. The former is dynamic work, and the latter is static work. And it often contains full of danger and spirit of sacrifice! You must be calm, careful, deliberate and agile, and be able to adapt to the situation. From my own observation; if you train novices, you must first let him or her know some important wartime common sense. If you are rich in common sense, you will not panic and be at a loss, and then use the concept of the country, the nation, and saving the country to encourage the spirit of sacrifice and bravery of the staff!"

"I admire the machine! This is really the happiness of the soldiers fighting against the enemy on the Suiyuan front lines!"

"Not to mention that the soldiers fighting against the enemy can really have someone to take care of them carefully, even if they hear a word or two to encourage them, they are very excited and moved. This has already given us an experience during the "January 28th". This time we will certainly make every effort, but sometimes I am also very

Page 20

Encouraged by the spirit of the strong men who worked hard on the front lines. Therefore, I believe that the current spiritual training is just a necessary procedure. If the staff arrives at the front lines, I believe that they can get incredible encouragement in spirit!"

"I heard that the puppet bandits are so brutal and unreasonable that even the rescuers may be targeted as attack targets."

"I have heard of the incidents of attacking Christian churches and killing church members. As for the rescue work, because we had already expected this, we had taken precautions in advance, so nothing unfortunate has happened."

"Yes, the newspaper also published that the church minister Yi Shifang commanded the church members to open earthen cannons to resist the enemy, and received Mr. Fu Zuoyi's praise!" I then said; "The current war on the front lines has probably moved to the eastern part of Suiyuan, right?"

"Now the enemy is scheming to covet the Hsingho area. Because the northeast there is adjacent to Zhangbei Shangdu. Zhangbei is the base of the puppet bandits, and it is the same as the conquered Bailing Temple before. The enemy also knows that the base of our army is in Shanxi, and the southern part of Hsingho is directly connected to the Great Wall and the gateway to Shanxi, Tianzhen Yanggao, and Jining is also nearby. The enemy's northern invasion has repeatedly retreated, and it is already hopeless to enter Baotou, then there is only one strategy to attack Hsingho."

Speaking of this, I saw that there were already many visitors, so I said goodbye and left.

Book and Newspaper Introduction

Introducing "War and Espionage"

— Kanfu

——Written by Rowan of England, translated by Hu Yuzhi, published by Shenghuo Bookstore, priced at three jiao per volume——

The world is on the eve of a great war, the smell of gunpowder permeates the whole of Europe and the Pacific Ocean, as long as a person with a little common sense knows that the threat of the Second World War is getting closer and closer to us every day.

At this time, in addition to striving for military competition, countries are also enthusiastically engaged in espionage warfare. In order to spy on the military secrets of other countries, in order to understand the activities of other countries' diplomacy, they spend huge sums of money every year, and use various clever methods to organize their own spy network. Therefore, although the war between countries has not officially broken out, the espionage war has already begun. As a result, many countries are suffering from espionage panic. Not long ago, Singapore did not crack a large espionage organization? And our friendly neighboring country in the east also discovered the sex scandal of American military officers using women to spy on military intelligence? Even a large-scale German espionage organization has been discovered in the Soviet Union. All of this tells us; the active state of espionage before 1914 has reappeared today.

Precisely because our world is full of espionage activities, legends, memoirs, novels, and treatises about espionage in European and American countries in recent years have become the most popular popular readings. "However, most of the works, because they cater too much to the vulgar psychology, are often detective novels, and even mythologized, and completely lose the value of history." Comparatively, only the book "War and Espionage" written by Rowan of England is worth recommending.

This book has recently been translated by Mr. Hu Yuzhi and published by Shenghuo Bookstore as one of the World Knowledge Series. The content is divided into fourteen chapters. The first chapter is "Modern War and Espionage". In this chapter, he first explains the relationship between modern war and espionage. He believes that "espionage has become an indispensable thing in modern war." "The biggest difference between spies and the military is that the military can only operate in wartime, while espionage activities do not distinguish between wartime and peacetime." At the same time, he also pointed out that espionage activities are a moral contradiction in the current society, which cannot be resolved at present. The second chapter, "The Development of Modern Espionage Systems", mainly explains the development of the independent science of espionage since Steib, Bismarck's famous detective chief, started working in 1870. The third chapter explains the basic principles of espionage work. Chapters four, five, six, and three are dedicated to discussing the information work of spies, the methods of transmission, and the issue of female spies. The author is very familiar with the espionage activities during the European War. Every time he explains something, he cites many extremely moving stories in history to elaborate. For example, how Germany deployed spies in countries such as Britain and France during the European War, how countries such as France and Belgium used extremely clever methods to transmit information, how British spies explored the sunken enemy submarines in the deep sea, how the Allied countries intercepted the German military codes, and various secret communication methods. In his narration, it is like listening to a legendary story, which is not only full of interest, but also makes people extraordinarily thrilling.

However, it is not enough to simply explain the work of spies. Because there is espionage work, there must also be counter-espionage work. "The so-called counter-espionage, on the surface, is opposed to espionage, but in reality it is not. If spies are responsible for offense, then counter-espionage is responsible for defense. Offense and defense are not opposite but complementary." In other words, counter-espionage is the spy of spies, and it can also be said to be a higher-level spy. Therefore, this kind of spy is more important in the current countries. This is also an important tool used by various countries to prevent spies from other countries and protect their own secrets.

Therefore, in the seventh, eighth, and ninth chapters, the author talks about the counter-espionage system in great detail, such as the history, methods, and secret police of the establishment of the counter-espionage system, the examination of letters, and the moving stories of all counter-espionage before and after the European War, which makes us read and learn about the methods of preventing enemy activities. At least we can get a lot of help.

Chapter 10 talks about "Propaganda", which talks about the method of using spies to spread rumors and incite military morale. The author also cites the story of the Austrian army using rumors to defeat the Italian army during the European War, causing the entire army of 500,000 people to suffer great losses.

In the last four chapters, the author is used to describe many spies who shocked the world in recent centuries. The first is Steib, Bismarck's detective chief, the second is Napoleon's spy Schulmeister, and the other is two famous female spies during the European War. "Miss Doctor" and the dancer Mata Hari, and the other is a famous spy in history, such as Defoe, the author of Robinson Crusoe, and Taion, an eighteenth-century spy, and he also described some reckless spies and their jokes, which are very interesting.

The author of this book, Rowan, has a great research on espionage. The historical materials collected in the book are also quite rich and precise. It is very important to understand the development of modern espionage systems and international espionage activities. Mr. Hu's translation is exceptionally fluent, and reading it not only does not make people feel that they are reading a translated work, but also feels like they are reading a novel.

However, this book also has considerable shortcomings. First, most of what he talks about are stories before and after the European War, and there is no mention of the current world espionage war. Second, there is no description of the espionage situation in the United States and Japan. Third, his national concept is too deep. Although it has been cut by the translator, his exposure to imperialism's oppression of small and weak nations and other aspects is still not sufficient. Even so, this book is still very necessary for our current China. Because, we are currently facing a serious national crisis, and imperialism is playing a great role in our espionage activities. Therefore, espionage activities and counter-espionage activities for the purpose of national self-defense are also what we currently need very much. Because this is an unarmed combat organization, we should not give it up. The publication of this book will undoubtedly give us a great help and inspiration in understanding this issue.

Essays

Street Art

— Lu Ren

The art that people usually notice is the Western paintings, watercolors, sculptures, reliefs, prints, and woodcuts displayed in galleries or exhibition halls, not street art. Little do they know that there are also our artists working hard to create their artworks at street corners.

In those humble and narrow streets and alleys—not on the magnificent Nanjing Road—we often see a group of children huddled together, surrounding a peddler with a shoulder pole making sugar figurines. In the minds of those artists, in the minds of those art connoisseurs, it is never considered that outside the "palace of art" there is also this nameless art... However, for ordinary poor children and impoverished people, they have their own art. The sugar figurine peddler on the street is the artist in their minds.

Strangely enough, using the same sugar, except for very simple tools, he relies entirely on his hands to make dozens of different things. In the short tens of minutes I observed, he had already made a turtle, a snake, a frog, a dragon, and a bird. According to him, he can not only make butterflies, fish, clocks, abacuses, mice, and other commonly seen objects, but also various characters, such as Guan Gong, Zhang Fei, and the like, just like Guan Gong and Zhang Fei appearing on stage in current opera troupes.

Our street artist understands history better than those who study history. He knows what kind of clothes those characters should wear, what weapons they should carry.

Page 21

He also fully understands the facial makeup techniques of old operas, knowing who should have a white face and who should have a red face. In his works, each character has a specific characteristic in their facial expressions, eyebrow and eye positions. Putting two Guan Gongs together, it's simply impossible to tell which is which. He can also create beautiful modern girls, and he can also create young men in suits and leather shoes. He can do anything he sees. He can make airplanes, trains, and ships. It seems that whatever is invented in the world, a similar thing can be found on his carrying pole.

Moreover, he understands general child psychology to cater to the minds of countless children. The things he makes must be what children like in their hearts. He can immediately create whatever a child asks for without hesitation. He can deal with children. He is not afraid of many children disturbing him, hitting him, squeezing him, snatching his sugar figurines, or hindering his work. He does not get angry and can handle everything with ease. When many children are vying for sugar figurines, he can make them take their turns without arguing. On one hand, he has to rush his work, on the other hand, he has to prevent children from stealing things, and on the other hand, he has to guard against patrols or police officers who come to drive him away. This is truly a world apart from the artists who sit in the "palace of art" and create artworks in peace.

He also sets up a grinding disc at one end of his carrying pole, asking children to bet on winning or losing with a copper coin, and giving them sugar to eat whether they win or lose. A carrying pole serves as a table, a counter, and a seat. He is very happy at heart, making artworks all day long, and also being with those innocent and lovely children. He is also a favorite friend of the children. This is also different from those bookish artists who are often complaining about "boredom" and "suffering."

In less than five minutes, I watched him make two snakes. The color of the snakes was celadon green. He skillfully blended green and yellow sugar together, just like a painter mixing colors, to create the color of celadon green snakes. A flat, round piece of sugar was stretched out in the blink of an eye, resembling a real wriggling snake. The patterns on the snake were printed with a broken wooden comb. This wooden comb of his is naturally less valuable than the comb that a modern girl takes out of her purse on a tram, but it is much more useful. It not only makes the patterns on snakes, but also imprints the fingers of people and animals, and can also imprint hair. The utility of a broken comb is truly beyond expectation!

The snake is coiled on a piece of cardboard. The head is the most complex and also the most interesting, with whiskers coming out of its mouth and two sparkling eyes. He can not only make various individual animals, but also, like a painter, combine various animals to achieve balance. A frog is placed in front of the snake, and the snake is looking at it as if to bite it, while the frog is like the angry frog encountered by King Goujian of Yue on the road, showing an unwillingness to submit.

This street artist is like the great French writer Guy de Maupassant. The subjects he depicts are small, trivial, and commonplace, readily available. There are also artists like this who make small toys, paint advertisements, and perform tricks. They are truly folk artists.

Vanguard of Aggression

— Jin Yue

There are many people in this world that we would never expect, and this friend whom I met for the first time is one of them.

I met him at a friend's house. He had just collapsed on the bed to smoke opium. After my friend introduced us, he looked at me with his nearsighted eyes. Probably because my friend had said a lot about me in front of him, which made him feel that I was someone who deserved his considerable respect—in fact, I was just a poor man who was incapable and had nothing—he suddenly put down his opium pipe, pinched his nearsighted glasses with his fingers, looked me up and down, and then said loudly, "Oh! Mr. Jin, please sit down. When did you arrive? We were just talking about you! Please sit down, have some tea. Business in Shanghai is not good! We were just talking about you! Please sit down, have a smoke." He said so much in one breath. He wanted me to sit down, have tea, and have a smoke, completely forgetting that I was just one person and could not split myself to do so many things at the same time. Moreover, in that chaotic situation, I didn't know what to say in response. I could only take off my long gown and repeatedly say, "Okay, okay, you pour, don't be polite, you drink, you smoke."

As if responding to an echo, he actually did what I said. He sat up, drank a cup of tea, and then collapsed back down to smoke.

My friend said to him, "Mr. Jin has lived in Xiamen for a long time and has worked in the press. He recently came from Beijing."

As soon as Beijing was mentioned, my friend whom I had just met put down his opium pipe and said to me, "Beijing, the emperor's capital, there's the emperor's palace."

I love Beijing, and I also love talking about Beijing with others. I briefly described the magnificent scenes in the imperial palace to him. Finally, I mentioned the imperial gold seals. "Like square inkstones," about ten or so, all gleaming gold.

Gold is moving, and he jumped up from the bed, shouting, "Ten or so? My god, wouldn't that be over ten thousand dollars?"

"Yes, the big ones must be worth tens of thousands of dollars," I nodded and said. But he did not just nod, but also shook his head desperately. After shaking his head, he sighed and said, "Beijing! Look! Beijing!"

He wanted us to look at Beijing, but what to look at? Everyone who has been to Beijing loves Beijing. There is the prosperity of the city, and there is also the tranquility of the countryside. But in his mind, Beijing only has ten or so gleaming imperial gold seals.

From the conversation about the imperial gold seals of Beijing, I roughly understood the hobby of my friend whom I had just met. And in the pervasive smoke, I also roughly recognized his appearance: a pair of rat-like nearsighted eyes, and a few messy short whiskers growing under a face that was so thin that it could not be thinner, and slender fingernails stained with opium.

When he left, he enthusiastically invited me to his house to play, and even offered to spare a room for me to live in. I thanked him one by one. I also followed my friend to see him out and said goodbye. I would very much like to have a detailed conversation with him again and would like to know how he lives in this world. From my friend's conversation, I knew...

Shanghai Postal Administration Mail Dispatch Schedule

All branches in Shanghai can send registered express airmail and handle remittances, savings, and other services.

Page 23

His surname is Wang, and he is the owner of a money shop.

Although he himself is very thin, he has a very fat mistress and a quite beautiful younger sister.

He also has several maids, who have now grown up and are very able to make money for Boss Wang. When the maids go out on errands, if there are wealthy customers, Boss Wang's mistress often follows behind.

Boss Wang is very good at helping the poor. People with financial difficulties can borrow money from his money shop. Borrowing one hundred yuan actually gets eighty-five yuan, with the remaining fifteen yuan as interest, for a period of one month, and one hundred yuan must be returned upon maturity. Boss Wang is a foreigner, and everything has backing. He is not afraid of people running away with his debts.

Boss Wang's residence is very spacious. The money shop is downstairs, and the mistress's bedroom is on the first floor. According to Boss Wang, because the second floor is a pity to leave empty, half of it is given to friends as a club. Friends gamble and smoke opium there, and Boss Wang can also get several hundred yuan in gambling commissions each month. The other half, it is said, is for the maids to play in. Boss Wang does not seem to care much about them, but when there are no guests to play with the maids, Boss Wang wants them to come to his room to smoke opium and make tea.

Therefore, Boss Wang is now very rich. According to what he himself tells people, he has close to ten thousand in assets.

A few days later, I saw Boss Wang again at my friend's house.

From his conversation, I also learned that he is a fan of gambling "Eleven Sticks." He said, "I dreamed of two pigs the night before, with two horns growing out of their heads, standing in front of my mother. Pigs are a black image, I bet on black image, bet ten yuan, and won."

I felt that Boss Wang would not tell lies. Someone like him should often have dreams. He would dream of demons eating people and also dream of wolves and tigers chewing his bones.

He said to people, "Bet! Starting from one yuan, one yuan wins ten yuan, then bet again, ten yuan becomes a hundred yuan, a hundred yuan becomes a thousand yuan, then bet again, a thousand yuan becomes ten thousand yuan, a hundred thousand yuan, a million yuan. Damn it, shut down all the twenty or so gambling dens in Xiamen, let us get rich."

One friend said to him, "If all thirty or so gambling dens are closed down, would Xiamen still be a good place to live? Each gambling den can at least support forty or fifty hooligans. Thirty or so gambling dens can support one or two thousand hooligans. If the gambling dens are all closed down, where will one or two thousand hooligans go to make a living? Your money shop might be in danger, and your women might not be able to take gold jewelry out."

Although this friend's political views are not very brilliant, our Boss Wang does not care about these things at all. He just says, "Bet! Everyone bet! Bet them into bankruptcy."

Boss Wang seems to have some past vendetta with these gambling dens. Later, according to my investigation, I learned that the original reason was that one gambling den refused to let him join as a shareholder.

One day, driven by curiosity, I actually visited Boss Wang with a friend.

In the money shop downstairs, I saw his fat mistress and his younger sister wearing a red cheongsam. On the second floor, I saw Boss Wang collapsed on the bed smoking opium.

As soon as he saw us, he immediately put down his opium pipe, invited us to sit down, and shouted loudly downstairs, "Hey! Brew a pot of tea."

We all sat down and talked a lot, but the tea had not yet been brewed.

"Hey! Brew a pot of tea, Tieguanyin, a lot of it. Buy two more chicken cakes and five bananas." Boss Wang continued to shout downstairs.

After five minutes, the tea and cigarettes still had not been delivered.

I thought that the mistress probably did not pay much attention to Boss Wang's instructions, and the maids upstairs just happened to be busy with business. There were sounds of playing cards upstairs, as well as the sounds of women and men laughing. Boss Wang would have at least a hundred or so dollars in income tonight.

But just as I was about to laugh, Boss Wang suddenly raised a question.

"Isn't it? Mr. Jin, I say that being a person requires benevolence, righteousness, courtesy, wisdom, and trustworthiness. We must believe in Confucius, Jesus God, Bodhisattva, and the Earth God, isn't it? Mr. Jin."

But at that time, I really could not answer this question to Boss Wang. In fact, Boss Wang did not need my answer, so I just asked, "What kind of dreams have you had these days, Boss Wang?"

Speaking of dreams, Boss Wang became even more energetic. He said loudly, "Yes, yesterday I dreamed of a pig again, unlucky, I forgot it as soon as it dawned, I waited until I opened the Eleven Sticks, it was a black image, then I remembered, really unlucky, I lost ten dollars yesterday, I can't win it back today."

"Oh! You dreamed of a pig again."

"Yes, strange, I often dream of pigs."

We seemed to talk a lot, but the tea and bananas still did not come. Boss Wang was probably angry because he needed to drink tea himself, so he was really angry. He knew that shouting for tea and bananas on the bed would not be effective, so he reluctantly got out of bed, pointed to the boils on his feet, and said to us, "Sigh! You see, two on the face, two on the feet, a total of four, boils, all boils, they hurt like hell, I didn't bring a flashlight last night when I went out, I bumped into a stone lion, it broke, and I bled two cups of blood, oh, it hurts like hell." Boss Wang said this and limped, limped to the head of the stairs, stretched his neck and shouted downstairs, "... Bananas!"

"I went to buy them, and I haven't come back yet! Why are you shouting so desperately?" The mistress was a little angry. So, Boss Wang, standing at the head of the stairs, remained silent for two minutes, and then limped to the bed, climbed up, and started smoking.

The tea and bananas were finally brought by the smallest maid. Boss Wang was angry at that moment. He took a bamboo strip and slapped the maid a few times, scolding, "You stinky x, x your mother, where did you go? Bastard." The tiger-like power was revealed in Boss Wang's short and messy beard. Boss Wang was indeed a bit heroic at this time.

After our intercession, Boss Wang finally let the maid go and went on to talk about his real business.

He asked me to do something for him.

According to Boss Wang, there was a sworn brother who did not care about morality and benevolence, and cheated his maid's jewelry to gamble. Heaven sometimes doesn't have eyes, and he happened to win money gambling, and he also bought a few maids to do business. Moreover, he happened to live next door to Boss Wang. According to Boss Wang, everything can be done according to the brotherhood and not be bothered with. It's just that these few maids are really stinky and cheap, and they often lure Boss Wang's friends upstairs over there, which makes it very difficult for Boss Wang. Because Boss Wang is very worried about his friends upstairs, these friends are very young, and if they are corrupted by those maids next door who Boss Wang thinks are stinky and cheap, wouldn't that be letting his friends down and losing faith? Therefore, he had to ask for my help. As for how to help, Boss Wang was confident about this. He said to me softly, "This is very easy for you, sir. He is not a real foreigner, and he has not obtained a license from the Chinese authorities. You just need to write a news report about him, and he will have to move away."

I suddenly realized that Boss Wang's tea and bananas were related to benevolence and righteousness. And at that time, I did drink Boss Wang's tea, so although I did not directly agree to his request, I could not help but wish him more accurate dreams so that he could win a few more rounds of Eleven Sticks.

In fact, Boss Wang did have a dream that night, but this dream was not a pig's head with two horns growing out of it, but a dog and a cat fighting.

The next afternoon, my friend said to me, "Boss Wang's mistress scolded Boss Wang a lot today because Boss Wang's dream was not accurate, which made her lose a lot of money."

Amateur Study

What Insect Researchers Need to Know About Making Their Own Insect Specimens

— Ziyun

I have a Western friend who is an insect expert, so he is very fond of making animal specimens for research purposes. On the four walls of his living room, there are almost all boxes of gorgeous butterflies, dragonflies, and many other kinds of beetles; everyone thinks this is more beautiful and meaningful than screen paintings and calligraphy. The following are the simple rules for making insect specimens that he told me.

Necessary tools: a pair of scissors, the tips of which should be sharp and straight, used to separate the various parts of the animal; a pair of tweezers, usually small and pointed, used to pick up objects, lest picking them up with fingers would cause contamination; a bug-stopping clamp; when sticking animals on the board, if you use your hands to press them in, it is easy to bend the pins, and when moving the specimens, it often damages the object, so use a bug-stopping clamp to hold the tip of the needle, either to pull it out or to stick it down, which is very convenient; a bug-catching net, used to catch insects; the net is two and a half feet long, the diameter of the mouth is half a foot, stretched with mosquito netting yarn, gradually shrinking from the diameter of the mouth into a conical shape, sew its mouth onto a steel ring, and install a wooden handle, four feet long, on the ring; two or three glass bottles, the most suitable being round with lids, containing a small amount of potassium cyanide, covered with a layer of cotton or cloth, which can be used as a poisonous bottle for raising animals; an insect-stabbing platform, made of wood, divided into two levels, each level has holes, which must be able to allow the insect needle heads to pass through; a set of wing-spreading boards, using a rectangular piece of wood, with the sides inward, leaving a groove in the middle, used to spread the wings of insects flat; if there is no such board, two rows of glass sheets can be stacked, leaving a groove in the middle; a humid insect container, using a large glass jar, containing about two inches of saturated moisture sand, and then adding a few drops of carbon disulfide and carbolic acid to prevent the growth of fungi; in the middle of the jar, place an iron wire mesh, and place the specimens to be taken to spread the wings on the mesh; if there is no such humid insect container, the wings of the insects will easily break, and the specimens produced will not be beautiful; in addition, some insect needles are needed. These tools can be made by oneself, and scientific instrument companies also sell them.

Necessary medicines: (1) Anesthetic, the most suitable being chloroform; (2) Preservative, alcohol is the best; (3) Antiseptic, camphor powder or camphor pills are the most commonly used.

The best time to make specimens is in late spring and early summer, because that is when hundreds of flowers are in full bloom and there are the most insects. Now I will try to divide the methods into several categories.

Regarding Lepidoptera, such as silkworm moths, swallowtail butterflies, nymphalid butterflies, etc., these are all, the specimens of this type of insect are exceptionally beautiful and interesting. To catch silkworm moths, you must go at night, first apply moth-attracting sugar on the bark of the tree, go to the tree under the light in the middle of the night, and you will see that there are many moths sucking on the sugar, so use a poisonous bottle to gently pick up the moths. After they are poisoned to death, use tweezers to clamp them out and place them on the wing-spreading board. The method is to put the body of the moth...
